And if *eastern sunrise* connects a dimmed node, it **explodes**: 1 armor destroying damage and prone to everything within 3 meters — and the node is no longer dimmed.

**3. Northern lights** — the first time each round you damage creatures with *eastern sunrise* or a *western sunset* explosion, choose one of them: it becomes a **star node**.

##### The Peacock Style

*Support*

Magnificent, flamboyant dancers on and off the battlefield — moving to a rhythm, be it cups on tables or swords on shields.

**Stance — Flamboyant:** when you taunt one or more targets, you regain 1 unphased. And the first time each round you move outside of your turn, you gain 1 temporary unphased.

**1. Deadly duo** — when you start or end your turn within 1 meter of a creature, you may take it as your **dance partner**:

- When one of you moves, the other moves too, staying within 1 meter — the follower spends no movement.
- You both gain +1 evasion against attacks from more than 1 meter away.

The dance ends if either partner is moved involuntarily, moves where the other can't follow (flight, say), is restrained or knocked out — or spends a move to bow out. One partner at a time; a new one replaces the old.

**2. Glorious step** — every stride, and every move through *deadly duo*, earns you a charge of **glamor**. When you finish your turn, you may spend all your glamor to **taunt** that many creatures that can see you. Losing your partner loses all your glamor.

**3. Precise tempo** — when one partner evades or guards, you may spend 2 glamor: the other takes the same move **for free**. And when your partner whirlwinds, 3 glamor buys them +1d12 to the attack roll.

- *Note: two peacock stylists can partner up. The benefits of* deadly duo *don't stack — but both earn glamor independently.*

##### The Spider Style

*Controller*

A web of invisible strings to restrict the enemy's movements — slowly creeping in, singling out your prey until it cannot escape. This is the way of the spider.

**Stance — Web:** on entering, choose a point you can see within 30 meters: it and the 3-meter radius around it become your **spider nest** until you exit the stance. And at the end of every round, you may place a **web token** on a creature you can see.

**1. Yarn spinner** — you gain a move, **connect strings**: on your turn, place 2 web tokens on a creature in line of sight. It can also be used as a **1-move interception** against a creature within 15 meters of **any of your nests** — pulling it to that nest's center. A creature pulled into the nest, or ending its turn there, is **restrained** for as long as it carries at least 1 token. Escaping tokens: *change the scene* and a power check — every success removes 2 tokens (0 successes still remove 1).

**2. Trapper of prey** — when *connect strings* pulls a creature towards your nest, you may pull up to **3 tokened creatures** 5 meters closer — and consume any number of their tokens for +5 meters of pull per token.

**3. Expanding web** — when placing a web token, you may spin a **new nest** centered on that creature. Up to 3 nests at a time; a 4th erases the oldest.

##### The Shepherd Style

*Commander, Support*

Developed by the farmers of the southern plains to keep their animals safe — its combat use came later, for its repositioning is unmatched.

**Stance — Wool:** while in this stance, any ally who moves (not pushed) outside their own turn gains 1 temporary unphased.

**1. Shepherd's guidance** — on entering the stance, and at the start of every round in it, you may move one ally closer to you by their **speed dice size** in meters (8, for a d8). If the ally is restrained, they shed the condition instead. An ally may refuse — then nothing happens.

**2. Herding sheep** — when an ally ends their movement within 1 meter of another ally, both count as being **behind soft cover** — until they part, or the round ends.

**3. The flock's figurehead** — when you stride, any number of creatures within 1 meter of you may follow your path **exactly**, regardless of their own movement speed. Hostile, restrained, unconscious and poisoned creatures cannot be herded.

##### The Brittle Steel Style

*Anti-striker, Versatile*

Born when a monastery sworn never to lift a weapon was attacked — a style of disarming enemies and unmaking their will to fight.

**Stance — Meditative:** until you exit this stance, you cannot make any hostile moves.

**1. Harmless retribution** — when a creature makes a hostile move against you and you neither guard nor intercept, it feels **intense shame**: −1 to its next resist roll within a minute, and its next hostile move within a minute costs you one less move to intercept.

**2. Shameful stalemate** — after a creature damages you or lands a condition on you, you may force it into a **willpower resist check** against your charisma or willpower dice count (+1 if your chosen attribute is a d10 or above). On a failure, its heart isn't in the fight: **−2 successes on all hostile moves** until the end of its next turn. Once a creature fails this, it is immune for the rest of the fight.

**3. Arm breaking pacifism** — when you intercept a move, you may **destroy one piece of equipment** the target carries. Mastercraft and legendary items refuse to break — they are instead knocked off, landing harmlessly at a point of your choice within 20 meters.

##### The Serpent Style

*Striker, Controller*

Created by a sect of master assassins — when one of them was sent to kill an entire platoon in a single night. A style of poison and swift debilitation.

**Stance — Toxic:** your first short reach attack each round inflicts **toxic poison** — the normal effects of poison, plus −1 to one attribute's rolls: speed, power, sense or endurance (chosen when you enter the stance). Removing it takes a move and an endurance check (test score 1); it fades on its own after 10 minutes.

**1. Septic shock** — when you hit an already poisoned creature, you may **end one instance of poison** on it and pick an effect:

- it makes 1 less move this round;
- it becomes **blinded**;
- it becomes **restrained** until the end of the round (test score 1 to escape).

Triggering septic shock also costs the target unphased equal to its own **endurance dice count** (+1 if its endurance is a d10 or above).

**2. Contagion** — when you inflict or end an instance of poison, you may pass that same condition to another creature within 10 meters. Triggered through *septic shock*, the range doubles.

**3. Potent poison** — *septic shock* against a **heavily wounded** enemy also costs it 3 resilience. And when *contagion* poisons a creature, you may immediately slither to within 1 meter of it.

#### A general note

The combat talents are divided into categories — but nothing stops you from combining weapon based talents with martial arts. It may well be *more* effective than sticking to one or the other (though some styles mix with weapons better than others).

### Magic based talents

#### General magic talents

These are talents all magic users can take at any point.

##### The Mana Manipulator

*Mage*

- *Special note: this is the **required** talent tree for using mana in even the most basic ways — no other magic based tree can be taken without at least 1 talent point invested here.*

**1. Beginner magic** — choose one of the 4 magic categories (Arcane, Occult, Holy or Natural) and gain the starting talent of that category. From now on, that category is your **chosen magic type** whenever other features refer to it.

**2. Efficient mana** — your grasp of the basics deepens your control: **+2 mana for every endurance die**, and your mana regeneration rises by 1 for every **willpower die**.

**3. Fledgling potential** — you learn 1 beginner spell. And from now on, every new spell you learn permanently raises your **maximum mana by 1**.

##### The Mana Adept

*Mage, Versatile*

Mana adepts push their manipulation to the next level — investing more mana to drive their spells beyond their normal limits.

**1. Heavy mana** — when you start casting a spell, you may invest an extra **2 mana** to enhance one aspect:

- the casting time drops by 1 (to a minimum of 2 moves);
- every creature affected by the spell takes 1 damage (regardless of the spell's effect);
- you gain +1 evasion until the start of your next turn;
- the spell's range is doubled (touch spells excepted).

**2. Empowered mana** — finishing a spell enhanced by *heavy mana* empowers you, whatever the spell did: you regain 1 unphased and gain **+7 meters of movement** for 1 minute, or until you start casting another spell.

**3. Mana engine** — the first time each round you spend any mana, you gain a charge of **stored power**. Spend it two ways:

- 1 charge — use *heavy mana* without paying the extra mana;
- cast a spell by spending an equal amount of stored power instead of mana (beginner and advanced spells only).

All stored power disappears when you regain mana.

##### The Sorcerer

*Mage, Versatile*

Master spellslingers who practice a unique art of casting — one that takes a heavy toll on the body, but weaves multiple spells at once.

**1. Multi caster** *(2 points)* — when you start casting a spell, you may pick a second spell of the **same level**, with an equal or lower casting time: it enters **twin casting**. Each move you spend progressing or finishing a cast while twin casting costs **1 extra mana** — miss a payment, and both spells fizzle. When you finish the main cast, you may pay the **combined mana cost** of both: if you do, both take effect.

- If you shorten or lengthen the main spell's casting time, the twin must match the *changed* time.
- The twin's own mana cost and casting time cannot be modified.
- The twin is untouched by your magic type's starting talent.

**2. Strained stress** — when you begin twin casting, you may take **2 damage** (ignoring damage reduction): if you do, the per-move mana payments are waived.

**3. Flexible casting** — your twin no longer has to match the main spell's level. And you may pick a twin with a casting time **1 higher** than the main spell — doubling the per-move mana payments (or raising *strained stress* to 5 damage).

##### The Student of Magic

*Mage*

Beginners and apprentices — a long road ahead before they understand the ins and outs of magic.

- *Special condition: requires the renown of an* adventurer.

**1. Compulsive study** — you learn **2 beginner spells**, and these specifically don't have to come from your own spell list.

**2. Novice spells** — you learn 1 advanced and 1 beginner spell from your chosen magic type's list.

**3. Graduation** — you learn 2 advanced spells from your chosen type's list, and permanently gain **+5 maximum mana** and **+2 mana regeneration**.

##### The Professor of Magics

*Mage*

Mages who finished their beginner training and cast advanced spells can deepen their study — and unlock their true potential.

- *Special condition: requires the renown of a* regional power *and a completed* Student of magic *tree.*

**1. Journeyman caster** — you learn one beginner, one advanced and one **master** spell from your chosen type's list.

**2. Calm mind** — once per day, spend 10 seconds (2 moves in combat) to gain **10 temporary mana**. Your maximum mana permanently rises by 3. And when you meditate, you may **swap out** one beginner or advanced spell you know for another of the same level from your list.

**3. Completed theses** — you learn 2 more master spells from your chosen type's list.

##### The Archmage

*Mage*

Few mages ever reach these greatest heights of mana manipulation — but those who do are remembered for ages.

- *Special condition: requires the renown of a* worldshaper *and a completed* Professor of magics *tree.*

**1. Power of the ancients** — **+7 maximum mana**, **+4 mana regeneration**, and the first spell you cast each round costs 1 less mana.

**2. Forbidden strength** — you learn one **legendary** spell.

**3. Unlimited casting** — after using *calm mind*, you may declare your next spell **unlimited**: it can be **any spell you know, no matter its mana cost**. Instead of paying orginal mana cost, you don't pay mana cost at all.

##### The Mana Artillery

*Mage, Sharpshooter*

A nickname for mages who specialize in long range casting and destructive magic — the kind that turns the tide of battle.

**1. Spell sniper** — the optimal range of ranged attack rolls made with spells can use your **casting attribute**, if it's higher (an occult mage with 2d10 charisma fires an ice spike at an optimal range of 20 meters). If you keep the normal optimal range instead, spells that use an attack roll deal **+2 damage**.

**2. Mana technique** — you may use **fighting techniques** on spell attack rolls.

**3. Prodigy casting** — choose one tree: **Sniper, Renegade or Spellshot**. You gain its first talent — and every talent of that tree can now affect spell attack rolls. (Renegade's *mobile shot* costs 1 mana to deal its 1 damage, and counts as casting a spell for your spell focus.)

##### The Junketeer

*Mage, Versatile*

Some mages abandon the weaker spells as they grow in power. Others appreciate what a beginner spell can do.

**1. Another man's treasure** — whenever you gain the option to learn a spell of advanced level or higher, you may learn **2 beginner spells instead** (3 for a skipped master spell, 5 for a skipped legendary). Beginner spells learned this way can come from **any category** — and spells from outside your list cost 2 more mana and 1 more move to cast. Spells learned through talents cannot be forgotten.

**2. Trash tosser** — when you cast a beginner spell you haven't cast since your last meditation, its base cost drops to **1** (a spell already at 1 counts as costing 0). For every **5 unique** beginner spells cast at a cost of 1 or less, all your spells deal **+1 damage** — the bonus resets when you meditate, and cannot exceed your casting attribute's dice count.

**3. Squeeze potential** — when a beginner spell targets a creature, pick one:

- the target gains 1 temporary unphased;
- its movement drops by 5 meters;
- it gains +1 success on its next resist roll this round;
- it is **poisoned** until the end of the round (test score 1 to remove).

##### The Summoner

*Mage, Commander, Versatile*

Masters of conjuration — invoking powers beyond mortal to command the battlefield.

**1. Conjured strength** — a creature you summon makes **2 additional moves** on its first turn. If one spell summons several creatures, they each make 1 additional move instead.

**2. Protective mana** — when you end your turn with at least one living summon, you may spend up to 10 mana: every point grants a summoned creature you control **1 temporary resilience**.

**3. Unlocked potential** — each type of summoning gains its own upgrade:

- **Spirit:** −1 more damage reduction (a −2 becomes a −3), +10 mana, and it regains 1 resilience at the start of each round.
- **Demon:** +1d6 to all hostile rolls, and it ignores immunities to the *fire*, *electric*, *frost* and *poison inflicting* tags.
- **Celestial:** allies it targets gain 1 temporary unphased — and **you** gain a flying speed of 15 meters (or +10 to an existing one).
- **Beast:** an additional move on its every turn.

##### The Bard

*Mage, Commander, Support*

Enchanters and performers who lace song and dance with mana — empowering allies and demoralizing foes through the power of sound.

- **Special ability — continued performance:** once per round, on your turn, spend a move to extend one melody until the end of your next turn.

**1. Songs of festival** — spend a move and **5 mana** to chant one melody (each lasts until the end of your next turn):

- **Melody of joy:** allies starting their turn within 10 meters of you gain +5 movement.
- **Melody of rest:** allies ending their turn within 3 meters regain 1 unphased.
- **Melody of glory:** allies starting their turn within 5 meters gain +1d6 to their next check.

**2. Songs of war** — two more melodies, at **7 mana** (each lasts until the *start* of your next turn):

- **Melody of victory:** allies starting their turn within 1 meter of you may remove 1 temporary negative condition.
- **Melody of protection:** allies within 10 meters gain −1 damage reduction and +1 evasion.

**3. Songs of lightning and thunder** — you learn **The Song of Storms** (12 mana, lasts until the end of your next turn): enemies ending their turn within 20 meters of you take 1 electric damage — and allies in the radius are immune to the *electric* and *frost* tags.

##### The Shaman

*Mage, Controller, Support*

Speakers to the spirits of the world — channeling them through totems, letting them reshape the field around them.

**1. Spirit medium** — spend 2 moves and 2 mana on your turn to raise a **spirit totem** (5 resilience, 0 evasion, −1 damage reduction; stands for 1 hour; you may keep several at once):

- **Totem of the eagle:** allies within 3 meters of it gain +1 evasion.
- **Totem of the rhino:** allies who stride and then attack a creature within 10 meters of the totem deal +2 damage on hit.
- **Totem of the turtle:** on placement, and whenever an ally ends their turn within 5 meters, they regain 1 unphased — after 5 total unphased healed, the totem shatters.
- **Totem of the beaver:** on placement, create up to 3 solid wooden pillars (1 square, 2 meters tall, 10 resilience, +3 damage taken from fire) anywhere within 20 meters of the totem — and one more at the start of every round.
- **Totem of the lion:** on summoning, every enemy within 15 meters and line of sight is **intimidated** for 1 round. And every time a creature is intimidated by any other source, the test score to remove it rises by 1.

**2. Unleash spirits** — when a totem is destroyed by damage, or when you spend a move to shatter it yourself, energy erupts from its place. Pick one:

- enemies within 5 meters are pushed 3 meters away;
- allies within 5 meters gain +1d6 to their next roll and −1 damage reduction against the next attack to hit them.

**3. Auspicious summoning** — you may raise **2 totems** for 3 moves and 5 mana. And when a totem is destroyed, you may spend 4 mana to immediately cast one of: *summon lesser land beast*, *spirit shield*, *lightning burst* (the totem counts as the caster), *lesser blight*, *lesser regeneration*, *ice spike*, *earth wall*.

##### The Undertaker

*Mage, Commander*

Undertakers perform the forbidden act of necromancy — raising artificial bodies of mud and clay, infused with mana: unnatural imitations of life.

- *Special note: all undead summoned through this tree act **last** each round, and count as **demons**. You may control multiple summons at once — as long as every summon you control comes from this tree. Your summons gain **+2 resilience per die** of your casting attribute, and add your casting attribute to all their rolls.*

**1. Corpse control** — you learn the beginner summoning spell **lesser necromancy** *(3 mana, 2 moves, 10 minutes)*: target a corpse of a creature that died within the last minute — it rises.

- *Risen corpse:* resilience 5, evasion 1, unphased 0, movement 10 m. Power 1d8, speed 1d6, endurance 1d12, sense/intellect/charisma/willpower 1d4.
- *Abilities:* **Persistent** — no negative effects from being heavily wounded. **Infected strikes** — its slam/slash damage poisons the target (cleared at battle's end, or when the target regains any unphased). **Cruel** — +1d6 to hostile rolls against restrained enemies. **Loyal** — it can never be intimidated, and never disobeys its master. **Minion** — only 2 moves, spent only on its own turn.
- *Hostile moves:* **Slam/slash** (short reach): 1d8, *brutal*. **Grapple:** 1d8 — restrains on a hit, deals 0 damage.

You may control up to **2 corpses** at a time.

**2. Corpse bloom** — spend 1 move to make one of your risen corpses **explode**: every creature within 5 meters takes damage equal to the corpse's current resilience. For each **heavily wounded** creature caught in the blast, you regain 1 mana.

**3. Master of the dark arts** — you learn the advanced spell **greater necromancy** *(9 mana, 3 moves, 1 hour)*: summon a vampire spawn, a skeleton elite, or an armored ghoul.

- *Base template:* resilience 15, evasion 2, unphased 0, movement 15 m. Power 2d8, speed 2d6, endurance 3d8, willpower/intellect/sense/charisma 2d10. **Persistent**, **Loyal**.
- **Vampire spawn:** speed becomes 2d10, power 2d4, evasion 4; it can **fly**, and gains *Vampiric strike* (short reach): 2d10 — *deadly, defensive, draining*.
- **Skeleton elite:** endurance becomes 3d4, base resilience 9, and it gains only **+1** resilience per casting die. Gains *Cursed warbow* (optimal 20 / max 300): 2d8 — *slow, armor destroyer, frost* — and *Cursed sword* (medium reach): 2d8 — *bladed, fire, electric*.
- **Armored ghoul:** power becomes 3d6, damage reduction −2, a heater shield (defense 2, 7 resilience, +1 resilience per casting die), and *Hammer down* (long reach): 3d6 — *brutal, forceful, armor breaker*.

Only **one** greater undead at a time — summoning a new one kills the old. And *lesser necromancy* now raises **2 corpses per cast**, up to 4 under your control.

##### The Collector

*Support, Versatile*

Eclectic, bizarre and strange trinkets. Tiny pieces of the self and others. Objects of unholy, alien and abhorrent influence. Collectors are safe harbors for such items — and strive to understand them fully.

**1. Forbidden keeper** — over a lifetime you've gathered a collection of tokens, and can draw on their power. When you meditate, you may **awaken** any number of them — your maximum and current mana drop by **2 per awakened token**:

- **Martyr's seal:** +1 maximum resilience (+2 if the wearer's endurance die is a d10 or above), and +1d6 to all rolls while heavily wounded.
- **Candle of life:** every time the wearer heals another creature, they heal 1 more resilience.
- **Hunter's talons:** +1d8 to ranged attack rolls against creatures with 0 unphased.
- **Swordsman's crest:** +1d12 to all melee attack rolls — but the wearer cannot heal others, and regains resilience only through the *heal up* camp activity.
- **Heaven's hairpin:** +1d4 to all rolls while in bright light.
- **Bloody dice:** the wearer's damage inflicts 1 rank of bleed — and attacks that hit the wearer inflict 1 bleed rank on them too.
- **Cursed incense:** −1 maximum resilience (−2 if the wearer's endurance die is a d8 or above); creatures get −1 success when resisting effects the wearer inflicts.
- **Shimmering scales:** −1 damage reduction — but +1 damage taken from all spells and mana-fueled abilities.
- **Virtue's chalice:** −1 maximum resilience; +1d12 on all intellect, charisma and willpower checks to resist negative effects.

Token effects don't stack from duplicates. All tokens fall dormant when you sleep — and your maximum mana returns.

**2. Broken promise** — when a creature wearing one of your tokens **would become Ashen**, they may **break the token**: they are reduced to 1 resilience and regain 1 unphased instead. A broken token gives no benefits or drawbacks (its resilience effects adjust the *maximum*, not the current value) — but still drains your maximum mana. You regain the broken token when you sleep, though it cannot be reawakened at your first meditation after.

**3. Divide the beyond** — choose one token: it is **always awakened**, and costs no maximum mana. And whenever a token breaks, you regain 1 mana and heal 1 resilience (the mana drain of the broken token still applies).

##### The Shaper

*Mage, Controller*

Shapers reach for the souls of living beings — mutating them, and killing them in the process.

**1. Cursed touch** — as a hostile move, touch a creature and pay 3 mana: it makes an endurance, willpower or charisma check (its choice) against your **casting attribute**. If you roll at least as many successes, inflict one of:

- **Burning rage:** the creature burns — 1 fire damage at the start of each round, until it spends a full round without making a hostile move.
- **Cold shoulder:** its speed drops to 5, until it helps an ally or casts a spell on one.
- **Toxic personality:** its allies starting their turn within 10 meters of it are poisoned for 1 round — until the creature takes damage.
- **Dark time:** it is **blinded** until an ally spends a move next to it to help (bypassing blinded's usual duration).

You may empower the touch: every **4 mana** adds +1 die to your roll (of your casting attribute's size). And resisting the touch hurts: the creature takes **2 unreducible resilience damage** even on a success — every **3 mana** spent adds 1 more.

- *Note: mana spent on one enhancement does not count towards the other.*

**2. Selfish change** — when *cursed touch* deals damage, you may siphon part of it into yourself, reducing the damage dealt:

- −1 damage: gain −1 damage reduction;
- −1 damage: +5 movement;
- −1 damage: +1 temporary unphased;
- −2 damage: +1 evasion;
- −2 damage: the next spell you cast costs 3 less mana (to a minimum of half its original price).

**3. Self perfection** — once per day, you may enter a **transcended state** for 1 minute: the mana cost of both *cursed touch* enhancements drops by 2 — and any effect of yours that requires **touch** works within **20 meters and line of sight**.

##### The Elemental Master

*Mage, Striker*

Those with a special connection to the elements empower the spells they cast — upgrading them to a whole new level.

**1. Profane soul** — you learn 1 beginner spell from the offensive elemental spell list. Elemental spells cost you 1 less mana (to a minimum of 1), and you may raise their damage by 1 — or by **2**, if the spell targets a single creature.

**2. Elemental surge** — casting a spell from the elemental category ignites a surge of hostile magic around you, lasting 1 minute or until you finish casting another spell: at the start of every round, you deal damage to all creatures within range, scaled by the level of the spell that started the surge:

| Spell level | Surge |
|---|---|
| Beginner | 1 damage, 5 m radius |
| Advanced | 2 damage, 10 m radius |
| Master | 3 damage, 15 m radius |
| Legendary | 5 damage, 30 m radius |

**3. Quick casting** — starting an elemental spell while a surge is active, you may end the surge prematurely to cut the spell's casting time by 1 (to a minimum of 1). Spells quickened this way count as **1 rank lower** for the surge they produce — so a quickened beginner spell produces no surge at all.

**4. Infused power** — you may switch the base damage tags of your elemental spells (one change per spell, even with multiple tags):

- **fire** → −1 damage, becomes **electric**;
- **electric** → becomes **frost**;
- **frost** → +1 damage, becomes **fire**.

Your surges carry the same damage tags as the spells that started them — switched tags included.

##### The Forgemaster

*Mage, Vanguard, Support*

Traveling blacksmiths, known far and wide for their proficiency in protection and enchantment magic.

**1. Hearth mender** — at the start of a round, you may spend 2 mana to enchant a suit of armor or a weapon within 1 meter of you (one enchantment per item; lasts until the end of the round):

- **Weapon:** gains a new trait, or swaps one of its traits for a new one (*armor destroyer* cannot be given this way).
- **Armor:** becomes immune to one damage tag: *fire, electric, frost, draining, condition inflicting, bleed* or *mana drain*.

**2. Gift of the fire** — when you meditate, you may cast one of the following without spending mana, with the duration stretched to **24 hours**: *flaming weapon*, *lesser strength*, *enhance armor*, *enhance weapon*, *light*. Up to 2 such spells at a time — a third ends the oldest.

**3. Adept smith** — you may use *smith & forge* **while traveling**, by working on it continually for 6 hours. And *hearth mender* can place **2 enchantments** at once for 3 mana.

#### Arcane magic

Users of arcane magic — also known as wizards — understand and manipulate mana masterfully: obliterating enemies with destructive spells, or granting supernatural abilities to their allies.

##### Starting talent: Deep study

You have learned the workings of magic and mana extensively. You can now learn spells from the **arcane spell list**, and when a spell requires a roll, you cast with your **intellect** (plus **double** the quality of your spell focus — the wizard's reward for understanding their tools). You learn **3 beginner spells** from the arcane list.

Arcane casting works through formulas and precise movement — bulky armor gets in the way: in anything but **high mobility** armor, all your spells take **+2 moves** to cast.

You also know how to extract the best from your focus — each grants an effect **on top of** its normal one:

- **Freeze focus:** when a spell of yours inflicts a negative effect, you may halve the target's movement until the end of its next turn. If the spell carries the *frost* tag — +1 damage instead.
- **Flame focus:** your damaging spells gain the *fire* tag; those that already have it deal +1 damage instead.
- **Electric focus:** single-target spells may deal 1 extra electric damage; spells already *electric* deal +1 damage instead.
- **Pure focus:** when the focus's attack hits, you may also deal damage equal to the mana the target lost.
- **Vampiric focus:** its trigger restores **3 resilience** instead of 1.
- **Sustaining focus:** you may also cut the casting time of a spell with a duration above 1 round by 1 move (to a minimum of 1).
- **Defensive focus:** you also gain +1 evasion until you take damage or your next turn starts.
- **Supportive focus:** empower up to **2 creatures** — or one creature for 2 rounds.
- **Conjurer's focus:** your walls also gain −1 damage reduction, and your summons +10 meters of movement.

##### The Chronagist

*Mage, controller*

Arcane casters who uncovered the secrets of time — and abuse them to skip ahead.

**1. Timeless mana** — when you start casting a spell, you may collapse its casting time to **1 move**, paying extra mana equal to **the spell's casting time +2** (a 3-move spell cast in one move costs 5 more mana). When combat ends, you regain 1 mana per use of this ability.

**2. Rewind** — when a single target spell you cast with a duration of 1 or more rounds ends, you may pay (3 mana for beginner, 5 mana for advanced, 9 mana for master and 15 mana for legendary) to **rewind time**: you cast the spell again, on a different valid target. You cannot rewind a spell more than once.

**3. Stopwatch** — using *timeless mana* now creates a **zone of stopped time**, 4 meters in radius around you, until the end of your next turn: entering it costs a creature a full move for a single meter of progress; ranged attacks automatically miss targets inside; melee attacks take −1 success. Spell effects originating from inside the zone only activate when it ends.

**4. Change of fates** — *rewind* may now re-target the **same creature**. Used this way, it costs the spell's original mana cost and creates a zone of stopped time.

**5. Time in a bottle** — when *timeless mana* or *change of fates* would create a zone, you may bank it instead as a **chronology charge**. You may spend charges at the start of any round: 1 charge — a zone lasting until the round ends; 3 charges — a **10-meter** zone lasting until the *next* round ends. All charges expire 1 minute after the last one gained.

##### The Scholar

*Mage, Versatile*

Wizards who copy their magic into spell scrolls — letting other creatures read, and cast, their spells.

**1. Spell cartographer** — you gain a camp activity, **scribe**: choose a spell you know and spend hours equal to its **mana cost** writing it down (the time can be split across rests and other activities). A finished scroll casts its spell **once**: 0 mana, 1 move to read. You maintain scrolls up to your **casting attribute's dice count** — scribing beyond that fades the oldest. A master spell takes up half your scroll slots (rounded down); a legendary takes them all. All your scrolls together occupy 1 inventory space.

**2. Empowered calligraphy** — casting from your scroll, pick one boost:

- +2d6 to the roll;
- a non-instant duration is **doubled**;
- a single-target spell also grants its target −1 damage reduction and +1d6 to its next roll for the spell's duration;
- +1 damage;
- a summoned creature gains unphased equal to the spell's mana cost (several summons — pick one).

**3. Learned scribe** — you may scribe **2 scrolls** at the same time.

**4. Expert scholar** — your scrolls survive **two** uses before crumbling.

**5. Arcane origami** — a scroll may be folded into a **living scroll** (single-use): flying speed 30 m, 2d8 speed and d4 in everything else, 1 unphased, 2 resilience, 3 evasion, 0 mana, 2 moves — it can only stride, evade, or cast its spell, either on its own turn or at your command (1 move from you).

##### The Trap Mage

*Mage, Vanguard*

Trap mages focus on canceling other magic users — preventing spells from ever taking effect, through anti-magic zones and magical traps.

**1. Spell trap** — you learn a beginner spell, **spell trap** *(2 mana, 1 move, 1 minute)*: choose a 1×1 meter square you can see within 20 meters — it is marked by an invisible trap. If a **magical ability** affects a creature touching that space, its effects are reflected back onto the original user (using the same roll, if there was one). The trap then ends.

- *A magical ability: anything that uses mana, or was acquired through one of the «immortal» enemy subtypes.*

**2. Mobile traps** — at the start of your turn, pay 1 mana to move an active spell trap to any visible point within 30 meters of you.

**3. Living trap** — spell traps can be placed **on creatures** instead of fixed spaces — lasting half as long. *Mobile traps* cannot target creatures.

**4. Double trouble** — when casting *spell trap*, spend an extra 3 mana to set **two** traps, on spaces or creatures in any combination.

**5. Anti magic trap** — you learn an advanced spell, **anti magic trap** *(5 mana, 1 move, 30 seconds / 2 rounds)*: mark a 3×3 meter square you can see within 30 meters. The first magical ability used within it is **canceled** — resources still spent. Then the spell ends.

##### The Specialist

*Mage*

Specialists devote themselves to a single spell — reducing its cost and pushing its abilities beyond reason.

**1. Specialized casting** — choose one spell you know: your **signature spell**. When casting it, you may pay extra mana equal to its level (beginner 1, advanced 3, master 5, legendary 9) per effect — paying multiple times buys multiple effects:

- roll your casting attribute — one target of the spell takes extra damage equal to the successes;
- the duration grows by 30 seconds (2 rounds);
- the target gains −1 damage reduction.

**2. Dedicated casting** — you may stretch the signature spell's casting time to improve it:

- **offensive spell:** every 2 extra moves → +3 damage (max +9);
- **single-target spell:** every 3 extra moves → +1 target within range (max 3);
- **anything else:** every 1 extra move → −2 mana cost (max −6; never to 0).

**3. Super-specialize** — you may immediately forget any spells that aren't your signature — and forget new spells the moment you learn them. Every forgotten spell yields **signature points** by level (beginner 1, advanced 2, master 3, legendary 5), spent on permanent upgrades (repeatable unless stated):

- **Versatile** *(the spell must deal damage or enchant equipment)*: gains a damage tag — fire (1 point), prone inflicting (2), electric (2), frost (3), blind inflicting (3), mana drain (4).
- **Maximum distance** *(must have an AoE)*: the AoE grows 1 meter. 2 points.
- **Bolstering** *(single target; once)*: the target gains a move on its next turn. 9 points.
- **Weaken** *(must inflict a condition; once)*: affected characters take −1 success on all checks on their next turn. 2 points.
- **Extend** *(duration of 1+ rounds)*: +1 round. 4 points.
- **Reduce cost:** −2 mana, to a minimum of half the original cost, rounded up. 6 points.
- **Empowered casting** *(single target)*: +1 damage. 3 points.

**4. Perfected form** — the signature spell's base casting time drops by 1 — down to **0**, but only if its original time was 1.

**5. Chant of the ancients** — casting your signature spell, you may begin a chant: the casting time (after all modifiers) is **doubled** (or +2, if it was 0), and you choose one:

- *«I desire for my torrent of power a destructive force without equal!»* — one target takes extra damage equal to the spell's mana cost.
- *«Blacker than black, darker than dark. I beseech thee, combine with my deep crimson»* — the spell now covers a **40-meter radius**; a single-target spell hits up to 4 targets instead.
- *«The time of awakening cometh»* — one affected creature gains +15 movement, +1 evasion, −2 damage reduction and +1d6 to all checks for 1 minute.
- *«Justice, fallen upon the infallible boundary. Appear now as an intangible distortion»* — the instant you finish casting, **end one spell** in your line of sight, before your own takes effect.

##### The Transporter

*Mage, Support*

Transporters wield the ancient magic of moving objects and creatures across great distances.

- *Special note: requires knowing at least 1 other advanced level spell.*

**1. Warp magic** — you learn an advanced spell, **lesser teleportation** *(4 mana, 2 moves, instant)*: choose an object or creature you can see within 5 meters (yourself included; no wider than 2 meters from its center, no heavier than 200 kg) — and transport it to a space you can see within **20 meters** of you. A creature must be **willing** — and a willing creature may lend its will to the magic, choosing its own destination instead: any space you can see within **40 meters** of you.

**2. Space swapper** — *lesser teleportation* may target **two** creatures/objects at once, swapping their places — if both are within 20 meters of you.

**3. Greater teleportation** — you learn a master spell *(7 mana, 3 moves, instant)*: you — or a creature/object you touched within the last minute (up to 10 meters from center, up to 10,000 kg) — teleports to a visible point within 30 meters of you.

**4. Mass transfer** — casting either teleportation spell lets you also shift **yourself** 10 meters in any direction.

**5. Dimensional door** — you learn a master spell *(10 mana, 4 moves, 1 minute)*: the space you stand on when you *start* casting becomes the **entrance**; a visible space within 2 meters of you when you *finish* becomes the **exit**. Anyone stepping through the entrance instantly appears at the exit. A creature standing on the entrance as the spell completes is teleported immediately; if the exit is occupied, travelers appear at the nearest safe space.

##### Arcane spell list

- **Defense:** anti magic.
- **Offense:** elemental, psychic, gravity, light.
- **Control:** illusions, terrain manipulation.
- **Summoning:** spirits, demons.
- **Support:** attribute enhancement, mobility options, equipment improvement.
- **Attack rolls:** intellect + double the quality of the spell focus you are using.

#### Occult magic

Occult magic users — also known as warlocks — control and command dark powers for great magical potential: bloody rituals, and the ability to fuel their spells with the vitality of the living.

##### Starting talent: Dark master

You gain the ability to learn and cast spells from the **occult spell list**, and can now take talents from the occult subcategory. When a spell requires a roll, you cast with your **charisma** (plus the quality of your spell focus). You learn **3 beginner spells** from the occult list.

Your magic is command over otherworldly things that live outside the world the great ent created. Because your power does not come from within — **armor does not restrict your casting**.

And because your spells rely on the powers of the beyond, you may tear a bigger hole in reality: each time you finish casting a spell, you may pay extra mana to **empower** it (one empowering effect per spell):

- **Summoning spell** *(+2 mana)*: the creature gains +2 resilience and +1d4 to all its rolls.
- **Damaging spell** *(+2 mana)*: +1 damage to all targets.
- **Spell targeting a creature** *(+1 mana)*: the target gains +1 evasion or +10 movement until the start of your next turn.
- **Range** *(+3 mana)*: +20 meters (doesn't affect melee attacks).
- **Duration** *(+4 mana)*: +15 seconds (1 round).

Every occult talent tree can also empower spells — and spells empowered **through talents** cost no extra mana.

##### The Blood Mage

*Mage, Champion*

Blood mages imbue their bodies with demonic energy — improving their physical and magical capabilities at the cost of their vitality.

**1. Demonic blood** — when you cast an occult spell **on yourself**, you may pay in blood: the spell is automatically **empowered**, and its mana cost drops by the damage you took (to a minimum of 1). The blood price scales with the spell's level: 1 damage for a beginner spell, +2 for every level above.

**2. Sanguine burst** — using *demonic blood* wraps you in a burst of dark energy: at the end of your turn it explodes, dealing every creature within 5 meters damage equal to the **total damage you took from demonic blood this turn**.

**3. Oni's blood** — you may take 1 extra damage before a *sanguine burst* activates to lace it with a tag: *frost*, *electric*, *continual fire damage*, or *blind inflicting*.

**4. Devil berserker** — while you are **heavily wounded**, *sanguine burst* gains *armor destroyer* and deals 2 more damage.

##### The Hellraiser

*Mage, Commander*

Call those who were forsaken and banished to the outer dimension — sacrifice your sanity to empower dark beings.

**1. Host of the rotten** — when you summon a demon, you may curse it with **mana-rot**: at the end of each of its turns, it loses 1 resilience or 2 mana (your choice, every time). In exchange, creatures your demon damages or targets with a spell are **poisoned** until the end of their next turn.

**2. Anti-priest of holy bodies** — whenever a demon you summoned loses resilience, all creatures within 5 meters of it take 1 damage. An **angel**, a creature mid-cast of a holy spell, or one under the effect of a spell you cast, takes **3 armor destroying damage** instead.

**3. Stitched, unholy homunculus** — when your demon dies, its remains linger until the end of your next turn: the area it occupied becomes **dangerous terrain** — and while you stand in the remains, all your spells are **empowered**.

**4. Chosen sacrifice** — your demon gains +1 success on all attacks and spells against **heavily wounded** creatures, and +1 success on resist rolls against effects such creatures inflict.

##### The Flesh Eater

*Mage, Vanguard*

Descendants of vampires, or practitioners of the dark arts — these dangerous occultists spend the blood of their enemies to fuel their spells.

**1. Blood feast** — when your spell damages a creature, your **next** spell this combat is automatically **empowered** and gains the *draining* tag. Damage dealt by a spell that already carries *draining* does not trigger this — and a multi-target spell counts as damaging only one creature for the tag's purposes.

**2. Bonestorm** — casting an empowered spell rattles the field: all enemies within 15 meters take 1 armor destroying damage — **3**, if the spell carried the *draining* tag.

**3. Miasmal shroud** — when you regain resilience, you exude an aura of poison and disease: creatures starting their turn within 5 meters of you are **weakened** until the end of the round. The aura moves with you and lasts until the next round starts — and every further resilience regained in the same round grows its radius by 5 meters.

**4. Deranged transformation** — ending your turn after damaging a creature with an empowered spell, you may transform: your movement speed becomes equal to your **current resilience** until the start of your next turn — and when the next round begins, you may stride without spending a move.

##### The Death Knight

*Mage, Controller, Commander*

Desperate folk who sold their soul for power — a twisted reflection of their former self, fixated on the one goal they gave their life for.

**1. Despair** — spend a move and 2 mana to summon a **shadow** in a free space within 30 meters: 1 resilience, no unphased, no damage reduction, your size, and it counts your charisma as its speed for evasion. Shadows take no turns — instead, if you took the *start casting* or *finish casting* move this round, each shadow may move 5 meters and deal **armor destroying damage** to one creature in its reach when the round ends, scaled inversely by reach: short — 5 damage, medium — 3, long — 1. You may control up to **5 shadows**.

**2. Gloom** — when you finish casting a spell, you may detonate up to 3 of your shadows: every creature within a dying shadow's reach is **restrained** (a move + power check, test score 1, to escape — +1 per additional exploding shadow overlapping the creature).

**3. Decay** — a creature damaged by your shadows, or starting its turn restrained by *gloom*, gains a **shadow mark**: spells you cast against marked creatures are automatically **empowered**. The mark is consumed by the empowerment (a multi-target spell consumes every target's mark).

**4. Desecrate** — when a creature starts its turn bearing a shadow mark, the ground beneath it becomes **desecrated**. At the end of the round, one of two things happens — and the desecration fades:

- a creature stands on the desecrated ground → it takes 1 frost damage;
- no one does → a **shadow** rises from it.

##### The Inquisitor

*Mage, Striker*

Feared warriors who wield their power discreetly — specialists of interrogation and single-target elimination.

**1. Marked for execution** — after you attack a creature with a weapon, you **mark** it: your next spell against it is **empowered**, consuming the mark. One marked creature at a time.

**2. Cruel judge** — your attacks against a creature that took damage from your spells last round — or is currently under a negative effect of your spells — gain *armor destroyer*.

**3. Quietus** — when an empowered spell hits a **heavily wounded** target and would deal it no damage, you may make it lose **2 resilience** anyway.

**4. Beheading** — when your weapon attack damages an enemy under the effect of a spell you cast, you may **end that spell**: the target takes damage equal to the spell's **remaining duration in rounds** (ending a restraining vine 2 rounds early — 2 extra damage). Against a heavily wounded target — double. An attack that triggers beheading still benefits from *cruel judge*.

##### Occult spell list

- **Defense:** Condition negation, anti magic
- **Offense:** Psychic, gravity
- **Control:**  illusion, inflicting negative conditions
- **Summoning:** demons, celestial
- **Support:** attribute enhancement, mobility options, healing, equipment improvement
- **Attack rolls:** charisma + the quality of the spell focus you are using.

#### Holy magic

Holy mages — or priests — pray to the mana surrounding them, and to the gods of the world, for the power to cast their spells. Serving the court of immortals and the new gods, their devotion grants them incredible strength.

##### Starting talent: True believer

You gain the ability to cast spells from the **holy spell list**, and can take talents from the holy subcategory. When a spell requires a roll, you cast with your **willpower** (plus the quality of your spell focus). You learn **3 beginner spells** from the holy list.

You cast through **prayer** — and every prayer is dedicated to a god. You must declare the god before starting the cast, and you must always dedicate to *someone*, even when the dedication adds nothing. Each god demands their own restriction, and grants their own gift:

| God | Restriction | Gift |
|---|---|---|
| **Julius Maxi**, he who stands firm | you must wear medium or low mobility armor | your barrier spells have their resilience multiplied by 1.4 (rounded up) |
| **Nazrha**, she of shattered teeth and blade | you must be heavily wounded, or have at least 1 creature intimidated by you | creatures you target become poisoned until they hurt another creature |
| **Himjle**, the ever curious and forgetful | you must declare the spell 1 round before you start casting it | one affected creature loses all damage reduction, or gains +1 evasion (your choice) |
| **Kalgara**, they who crave flesh and all-consuming lust | you must have regained unphased or resilience in the last minute | all affected creatures clear 1 condition of their choice |
| **Vilim**, of 10,000 epithets and no truths | you cannot cast the same spell twice between rests | the casting time drops by 1 (minimum 1), the mana cost rises by 1 |
| **Aom**, painter of the great beyond | the casting time rises by 1 | the spell's area of effect grows by 5 meters |
| **Yagsoloth**, the two-faced guardian-destroyer | spells cast on odd rounds are *dawn* spells; on even rounds — *dusk* | *dawn:* you and affected allies gain +5 m movement until the round ends; *dusk:* affected creatures who moved this round take 1 frost damage when it ends |
| **The Husk**, collector of ash and dust | you witnessed a creature die or become Ashen in the round you start casting | choose one Ashen creature you see: it **cannot die** until the start of its next turn |

Lastly, a quick prayer of yours cures weak diseases and heals small wounds (nothing that actually lowered unphased or resilience) — and you can bless water into **holy water**: an ingredient for some potions, or a healer's aid granting +1d10 to a first aid roll. One bottle at a time.

##### The Preacher

*Mage, Support*

Priests who support large groups of allies at once — or debuff crowds of enemies.

**1. Holy sermon** — casting a single-target support or control spell, you may spend one extra move to affect **two creatures** within a radius around you instead: 5 meters for a beginner spell, +5 per level above (advanced 10, master 15, legendary 20). Healing split between two targets gives each **half** the original amount (rounded up).

**2. Empowered beliefs** *(2 points)* — when a support spell of yours affects a creature, you may **empower** it: +1d8 to all its rolls until the spell affecting it ends. A multi-target spell empowers only one.

**3. Divine aid** — casting a support spell through *holy sermon*, you may also remove one negative condition from each target — or, if you don't, each recovers 1 unphased.

##### The Paladin

*Mage, Champion*

Warrior priests — attacking in prayer, smiting their enemies with holy power.

**1. Prayer of battle** — once per round, when you take the *finish/progress casting* move, you may also make a **hostile move for free**. Using it forbids attacking with a regular move this turn — and having already attacked forbids using it.

**2. Smite the heretic** *(2 points)* — an attack made through *prayer of battle* as you finish a cast gains **+2 damage** and one tag of your choice: *fire*, *blind inflicting*, *mana drain*, or *intimidation inflicting* (test score 2 to remove).

**3. Mark of the saints** — the first time each combat you become **heavily wounded**, you may claim one mark:

- **Mark of the martyr:** when an ally loses resilience, you may move 10 meters towards them — reaching within 1 meter restores them 1 unphased.
- **Mark of the merciful:** whenever you could use *prayer of battle*, you may **recover 1 mana** instead.

##### The Bishop

*Mage, Commander*

Bishops call upon their holy power to summon mighty creatures — and to empower those summons with magic.

**1. Heaven's ward** — when you summon a celestial, gift it one blessing (lasting until it disappears, or until you summon through a different spell):

- **Shield:** the first damage it would take is reduced to 0.
- **Gavel:** +1 die on its hostile moves (the largest die, if it uses several sizes) and +1 damage.
- **Horn:** its non-hostile moves may target one more creature.
- **Wings:** it can fly — or gains +10 movement, if it already could.

**2. Banishment** *(2 points)* — when a creature reduces your summon's resilience, or dispels it with magic, you may punish it: immediate damage equal to the summon's level (beginner 1, advanced 2, master 5, legendary 9) — **doubled**, if the damage lands on unphased.

**3. Call of the high king** — casting any celestial-summoning spell, you may conjure a **copy** with identical stats. When either the original or the copy loses unphased or resilience, the other loses the same — without triggering *banishment* twice.

##### The Devoted

*Mage, Versatile*

Those who dedicate their life to one of the new gods — working, preaching, advancing their agenda. Their faith shows even in their spells.

**1. Ceremony** — when you meditate, you may dedicate one spell you know to your god: it counts as **always cast under that god's restriction** (a barrier spell castable without heavy armor, say). After one cast, it locks until you sleep or meditate.

**2. Complete prayer** *(2 points)* — choose one god, forever: every spell you cast is now a prayer to them. If you begin a prayer and cannot meet the restriction, you take **2 unreducible damage** instead. In exchange, prayers your god accepts carry an empowered gift:

- **Julius Maxi:** creatures damaging your barriers take damage by the barrier's level — beginner 1, advanced 3, master 5, legendary 6 armor destroying.
- **Nazrha:** creatures poisoned by your spells risk going **berserk**: at the start of their turn, roll a d6 — on a success, they must try to hurt the closest available target.
- **Himjle:** casting a spell reveals all hidden creatures, traps and pathways within 20 meters of you.
- **Kalgara:** creatures you target with spells gain 2 temporary unphased.
- **Vilim:** if your last spell came from a different category, you may learn a new beginner spell of the *current* category (forgotten when you rest).
- **Aom:** an instant AoE spell may become a **star sign** for +1 casting move: it casts itself **again** at the end of the next round. One star sign at a time.
- **Yagsoloth:** *dawn* spells let every target immediately move 10 meters; creatures taking frost damage from *dusk* spells become weakened for as long as the *frost* tag reduces their movement.
- **The Husk:** you gain a new option when finishing a cast — target an **unconscious** creature and force it into the Ashen state (this does **not** count against its Ashen entries between rests).

**3. Bond of faith** — every prayer your god accepts earns a **faith token**. You may recast your *ceremony spell* paying in tokens instead of mana — each worth 3 mana (rounded up in tokens: an 11-mana spell costs 4). Casts paid in faith produce no faith.

##### The Shrine Keeper

*Mage, Vanguard*

A holy mage of talismans — consecrating the ground in preparation for powerful rituals.

**1. Protective seal** — when a round starts, pay 2 mana to place a **holy seal** in a free space within 2 meters of you (or place one as a move, free of mana). When a round ends, you may extinguish existing seals within 10 meters of a creature to cast a spell on them **without paying mana**:

- *Spirit shield* — 3 seals. *Gravity surge* — 2. *Lesser grit* — 4. *Partial invisibility* — 3. *Innocent fog* — 2 (the target counts as the caster).

Spells cast through seals are untouched by *true believer*.

**2. Temple overseer** *(2 points)* — casting on a creature through *protective seal*, you may consecrate a 10-meter radius around the target as **holy ground** (one at a time; +3 meters of radius per die of your casting attribute). Creatures standing on holy ground **count as holy seals** — and standing on it yourself unlocks more seal-spells: *Force cloak* — 4 seals, *Elemental shield* — 3, *Guardian spirit* — 5, *Armored mind* — 4.

**3. Sealed potential** — spending an **enemy** on holy ground as a seal restrains it until the end of the next round (test score 2 to escape). Spending an **ally** removes one temporary negative condition from them.

##### Holy spell list

- **Defense:** barrier and wall creation, resisting damage, negation of conditions, anti magic.
- **Offense:** light magic.
- **Control:** inflicting negative conditions.
- **Summoning:** celestials, beasts
- **Support:** attribute enhancement, healing, equipment enhancement.
- **Attack rolls:** willpower + the quality of the spell focus you are using.

#### Natural magic

Mages who use natural energy — druids — are so in tune with nature and mana that they sense it directly, feeling the essence of the creator Teragamalt echo around the world.

##### Starting talent: Nature's call

You gain the ability to cast spells from the **nature spell list**, and can take talents from the natural magic subcategory. When a spell requires a roll, you cast with your **sense** (plus the quality of your spell focus). You learn **3 beginner spells** from the nature list.

Your casting flows through your connection to your immediate surroundings — armor muffles it: in any armor, your spell rolls take **−1** and all spells cost **double mana**. Unarmored, your spells' casting times drop by your **sense dice count** (to a minimum of 2 moves).

Lastly, you can communicate emotions and simple ideas to animals — and understand their ideas and intentions in return — within 10 meters.

##### The Sprout

*Mage, Commander*

Druids who master spirit summoning — calling on the ancient spirits of nature to raise their magic and elemental power.

**1. Friend of the spirits** — you learn *summon lesser fey* (or another beginner spell, if you know it already). Spirits you summon gain **+4 mana per sense die** you have, and add your sense dice to all their spell-related rolls.

**2. Deep bond** — spirits you summon gain bonus evasion equal to your **sense dice count** while within 10 meters of you. If a spirit you summoned takes damage, you regain 1 unphased. When you take damage, spirits you summon may move up to 5 meters closer to you.

**3. Harness power** — when you finish casting a spell, you may cast it **from the spirit's position** instead of yours — and the fey may then start casting a spell of its own (2+ moves to cast). Likewise, when a spirit you summoned finishes any spell, you may start casting a 2+ move spell.

##### The Wild Lord

*Mage, Commander, Champion*

Wild lords change their form, summon beasts — and enhance their summons through their bond with magic.

**1. Chimeric transformation** — you gain a new move, **transform**: choose one or more **bestial enhancements**, each paid for in maximum mana:

- **Primal strength** *(−6 max mana)*: +1 power die.
- **Superhuman reflexes** *(−5 max mana)*: +2 speed dice size.
- **Durable hide** *(−5 max mana)*: +1 temporary resilience per endurance die, lasting until you exit the transformation.
- **Dense muscle** *(−8 max mana)*: +20 meters of movement.
- **Underwater adaptation** *(−7 max mana)*: waterbreathing, +10 movement underwater, +1d12 to all underwater rolls.
- **Toxic appendage** *(−7 max mana)*: your unarmed strikes gain *poison inflicting* (1 round; −1 to the target's sense, intellect and speed checks).
- **Wingspan** *(−30 max mana)*: you gain the ability to **fly**.

Primal strength, superhuman reflexes, durable hide and dense muscle can be taken **repeatedly**, paying each time. The transformation lasts until you rest, become Ashen, or spend 3 moves to exit; exiting restores your maximum mana, but not your current. Exit by Ashen locks transformation until you rest.

**2. In tune with nature** — transforming grants you temporary mana — **3 per sense die** (5, if your sense die is a d8 or above) — usable only for **beast summoning, damage resistance and light magic** spells. It lasts until you rest or exit the transformation.

**3. Born to be wild** — beasts you summon while transformed gain **all bestial enhancements** currently affecting you.

##### The Disaster

*Mage, Striker, Controller*

Disaster druids channel the destructive side of nature — volcanoes, typhoons, earthquakes.

**1. Ruiner** — the ground affected by your area spells becomes **harsh terrain** — and creatures starting their turn on any harsh terrain you created take 1 damage.

**2. Empowered destruction** — when your spell damages a creature, you may knock it **prone** — or push it 5 meters back and **intimidate** it (test score 1 to remove).

**3. Elemental mastery** — your damaging spells with the *electric*, *frost* or *fire* tag **ignore immunities** to that tag. And your non-damaging spells may inflict **1 continual damage** on everyone affected (removable by *change the scene*, or by regaining any resilience).

##### The Sea King

*Mage, Controller*

Some druids are bound to the push and pull of the waves — their magic swelling and ebbing as battle rages.

- **Unique mechanic — the tides:** even-numbered rounds are **high tide**; odd-numbered rounds are **low tide**.

**1. Ebb and flow** — starting a cast during **low tide**, you may pull a creature in line of sight closer to you by the spell's **mana cost** in meters. Finishing a cast during **high tide**, you may damage everyone within 5 meters of you — equal to the **moves the cast took**.

**2. Rising tide** — creatures you pull or push during low tide may also be knocked **prone**. And all damage from *ebb and flow*, and from spells cast during high tide, gains the **frost** tag.

**3. Tyrant's torrent** — at the start of your turn, pay 4 mana to raise a **whirlpool**, 10 meters in radius around you:

- low-tide casts now pull up to **5 creatures**;
- high-tide *ebb and flow* damage hits **everyone in the whirlpool**;
- raised during low tide, allies inside gain +1 evasion; during high tide — you gain −1 damage reduction.

The whirlpool lasts until the start of the next round of the **same tide** it was born in.

##### The Windrider

*Mage, Striker*

Druids of the open sky, drawing power from the wind whipping around them — chosen by the air itself, freed from the tethers of the land.

**1. Updraft** — finishing a cast gathers a small wind beneath you: you can **fly** until the end of your turn.

**2. Windfury** — casting a mobility spell earns you a stack of **fury** — and spending altitude for movement earns half the altitude spent (rounded up). Ending your turn, you may release all fury as a **whirlwind** around you, its radius equal to the stacks spent: it stays in place, counts as harsh terrain for everyone else, grants creatures inside +2 evasion against ranged attacks, and lasts until the start of your next turn.

**3. Free bird** — raising your whirlwind, you may push all enemies horizontally until they stand 1 meter outside it — and you regain **1 move and 1 unphased**.

##### Nature spell list

- **Defense:** barrier and wall creation, resisting damage, negation of conditions.
- **Offense:** elemental magic, light.
- **Control:** illusions, terrain manipulation, inflicting negative conditions.
- **Summoning:** beasts, spirits.
- **Support:** mobility options, healing.
- **Attack rolls:** sense + the quality of the spell focus you are using.

## General Talents

General talent trees cover everything from assisting travel to negotiating better prices — the broadest category of them all.

### Travel based talents

These trees improve a character's ability to travel — or expand what a character can do on the road.

#### The Squire

*Support*

Squires maximize and maintain the quality of the party's equipment. A good squire is never unnoticed — and always appreciated.

**1. Fast worker** — the *maintain equipment*, *polish armor* and *repair shield* camp activities take you **half the time**: twice the work in the same hours.

**2. Carry specialist** — +2 total inventory; long reach weapons and big shields cost only **1 space** to carry; armor and ammo cost 1 less.

**3. Tender care** — your three maintenance activities gain upgrades (lasting 24 hours):

- *Maintain equipment:* spend double the time — the weapon gains an extra +1d6.
- *Polish armor:* spend 1 extra hour — +1 defense value.
- *Repair shield:* also either +2 resilience, grant *sturdy (1)*, or raise an existing *sturdy* by 1.

#### The Wanderer

*Support, Versatile*

Expert travelers who have crossed the world — dangerous terrain included — with ease.

**1. Persistent step** — you **double** the hours you can travel, when moving at half speed or slower.

**2. Multitasker** — you may run **two traveling activities** at once, as long as neither is *camping on the go*.

**3. Well traveled** — when you take the *scout ahead* traveling activity, your presence carries the group: allies traveling along the wanderer also gain the benefit of *persistent step*, and they may use **your speed** instead of theirs when calculating travel time.

#### The Hunter

*Versatile*

Hunters are the best at surviving in the wild for long stretches — and can track creatures across vast distances.

**1. Tracker** — +2d6 to the *tracking* traveling activity. And when searching for food, every success feeds a total of **3 sizes**.

**2. On the move** — you may switch traveling activities **every hour** — or switch to full speed instead. You only enjoy the benefits of your *current* activity, but camp-enhancing effects keep their listed duration.

**3. Terrain expert** — the peak of blending in and reading the land. The *tracking* activity upgrades for you: the test score drops by 1 for every **3 creatures** in the tracked group.

- *An additional resting benefit is still in development.*

#### The Camper

*Support, Versatile*

Campers care for others — keeping the whole group in top shape.

**1. Caretaker** — your *raise morale* grants **+2d8** instead of +1d10. And if you spend the group's rest on *raise morale* or *heal up*, you only need **4 hours of sleep**.

**2. Helper** — dedicate your camp time to one creature: with your help, it completes its activity in **half the time**.

**3. Cozy camper** — your cheer heals: everyone participating in your *raise morale* regains **2 resilience or 5 mana** (once per creature per 24 hours).

#### The Guard

*Vanguard, Support*

Guards are vigilant — noticing the smallest detail when it comes to hidden foes.

**1. Watchmen** — keeping watch for at least 6 hours, you need only **2 hours of sleep**. And if battle starts, you may wake every sleeper by shouting as it begins.

**2. Keen eye** — +1d10 to sense rolls during *keep an eye out* and *keep watch* — and you are **immune to the unaware condition**.

**3. Always watching** — while traveling, whatever your activity, you also enjoy *keep an eye out*; while camping, you always count as keeping watch. (The other Guard talents still require choosing *keep watch* properly.)

#### The Cook

*Support, Versatile*

Masters of the culinary arts — keeping allies in top shape through delicious, nutritious meals.

**1. Chef** — you gain a camp activity, **cooking up a meal** *(1 hour; requires food)*: choose any number of creatures, spending 1 ration per creature (a ration equals the creature's size). Everyone who spends 30 minutes eating your food gains **+1d6 to power and endurance checks** for 12 hours — and counts as fed this rest.

**2. Calming cuisine** — creatures who sleep within 8 hours of eating your food recover up to **4 mana or 1 resilience** extra.

**3. Expert cook** — *cooking up a meal* now spends 1 ration per **2 creatures** — and your food also grants **+1d6 to speed checks and −1 damage reduction** for those 12 hours.

#### The Athlete

*Versatile*

Athletes push their bodies to the limit — performing almost superhuman feats of strength and agility.

**1. Trained body** — +1 success on checks to climb, swim, run, or perform acrobatic and athletic maneuvers (never on hostile rolls).

**2. Inhuman performance** — +5 meters of movement while you are not heavily wounded. And checks to remove impairments affecting power, endurance or speed treat the test score as 1 lower.

**3. Constant improvement** — *training an attribute* grants you an extra 1d6 — to the trained attribute, or another of your choice.

#### The Center

*Support*

Some feel more comfort resting in a familiar place. Some have the talent of making the most uncharted places feel familiar.

**1. Deep sleep** — creatures who sleep within your line of sight pick one benefit for the next 24 hours:

- benefit from one additional damage reduction effect;
- +1 base evasion (only in medium or low mobility armor);
- the first *intercept* each combat costs 1 less move;
- the first *guard* each combat costs no move.

**2. Pleasant dreams** — if sleep is your **first** camp activity, you double the mana and resilience regained from camp activities.

**3. Reinvigorate** — you gain a camp activity, **sacred grove** *(1 hour)*: a calming area, 15 meters in radius. Creatures sleeping in it gain the full benefits of sleep in **half the time**.

#### The Agent

*Support*

Professionals who learned to move undetected over long distances — and to guide others unseen through enemy territory.

**1. Undercover** — you may use the *cover tracks* or *lay low* traveling activity while traveling at **full speed**. And at half speed, you count as **2 creatures** when calculating the bonuses and penalties of either activity.

**2. Well trained informant** — when another creature attempts to hide within 10 meters of you, choose one — even if your character isn't actively aware of the attempt:

- immediately call out its location to every ally that can hear you;
- grant it **+2d6** to the roll.

**3. Pass without trace** — when a creature succeeds in locating you — or someone who benefited from *well trained informant*'s bonus dice — you or your beneficiary may immediately move up to **15 meters**. End that movement outside the seeker's line of sight, and they must repeat the check (the repeat cannot trigger this movement again). After moving this way, the test score to discover you drops by 1.

### Utility talents

Utility talents each focus on a specific profession, thing or set of actions — and improve it as far as it will go.

#### The Healer

*Support*

Healers are proficient in medicine and the ways of recovery — mending most wounds and illnesses.

**1. First aid** — on your turn, *change the scene* to treat yourself or a creature within 1 meter: roll an **intellect or sense check** — every success heals 1 resilience. Only works on creatures that have not been **Ashen** since their last rest, and were wounded within the last 10 minutes. One first aid per creature per rest.

**2. Practiced medic** — your *heal up* camp activity restores **2 resilience** instead of 1 — and may also remove one non-magical negative condition from the patient.

**3. Fast treatment** — once per 24 hours, heal up to **3 resilience** to an unconscious creature within 1 meter (sleeping counts).

**4. Miracle worker** — *first aid* also grants the target **2 temporary resilience**. And creatures you *heal up* can benefit from it again after **12 hours** instead of 24.

#### The Merchant

*Support*

Proficiency in trade and money is a valuable skill — especially on the road.

**1. Monetary negotiation** — the first time you *haggle*, you may cut the inventory point cost of **another item** by 1. And your group regains **2 more inventory points** from *acquire connections*.

**2. Valuable prospects** — every time you or your group uses an item someone haggled for, the user regains **1 inventory point**.

**3. Emergency funds** — you gain a camp activity, **refund** *(1 hour)*: you squeeze extra value from your goods. You or an ally regains **3 inventory points** — but the next time you'd regain points, you get **2 fewer**.

**4. Exquisite collections** — choose two common consumables, weapons or shields that cost 1 inventory point: they now cost **0** for you to use or equip (a chosen heater shield takes no inventory; a chosen poison dart is free to produce). You cannot sell items produced this way.

#### The Inspector

*Very versatile*

Inspectors specialize in uncovering hidden details — and hidden enemies.

**1. Keen mind** — +2d10 to checks made to understand a creature or object's properties and traits, or to recall information you once knew. Spend 1 move (5 seconds out of combat) to probe an enemy: the Qg reveals 1 of its abilities. The target may negate this with a contested charisma or intellect check.

**2. Sharp eyes** — +1 success on all checks to uncover hidden details, or to notice a creature hiding in your presence.

**3. Mindful gaze** — when checking someone's motives or hidden intentions, the lowest you can roll is **2 successes**.

**4. All seeing** — the test score to stealth within your line of sight rises by 3, and can never drop below 3. And *keen mind* can no longer be negated.

#### The Fraud

*Versatile*

Masters of disguise, breaking into places in plain sight.

**1. Sharp dresser** — you may add your **intellect** to any non-intellect check made to convince people using a disguise or your looks. If the check already uses intellect, add +1d8 instead.

**2. Crafty forger** — +2d8 to checks made to recreate an item you saw in the last 12 hours, or to improvise an item that helps you deceive.

**3. Quick mimicry** — +1d10 when passing yourself off as another person, or mimicking a creature's mannerisms.

**4. Fast excuse** — when a creature isn't fooled, you may immediately **reroll** the check. Either way, that creature becomes **cautious** towards you.

#### The Alchemist

*Support, Controller, Versatile*

Alchemists brew potions of unique and powerful effects — and invent wholly new concoctions.

**1. Alchemical brew** — you learn to brew with incredible efficiency. An **alchemical brew** takes 3 hours, brewed in one sitting through *craft an item*; you hold up to **3** at a time. Choose the effect on creation:

- **Spider lily:** the drinker climbs at full movement speed, no check needed — 2 hours.
- **Vigor brew:** −1 damage reduction — 2 minutes.
- **Spicy mix:** immunity to continual fire damage — 1 hour.
- **Iced drink:** immunity to the frost effect — 1 hour.
- **Energized drink:** +10 movement — 10 minutes.
- **Revitalizing brew:** +2 temporary unphased — 1 minute.
- **Electric drink:** immunity to the shocked condition — 1 hour.
- **Nightmare howler:** the drinker immediately **intimidates** all creatures within 5 meters for 3 rounds.
- **Acidic cask:** on shatter, everything within 1 meter takes **2 continual damage**.
- **Frosted cocktail:** on shatter, terrain within 4 meters becomes harsh terrain, and caught creatures lose 5 movement for 1 minute.
- **Enchanting aroma:** on opening, creatures within 5 meters make a willpower or endurance check (test score 2) — **weakened** for 1 minute on a fail. Usable twice; if shattered, it spends all charges at once for double radius and +1 test score.

**2. Alchemic savant** — your potions gain enhanced effects: drinkers also regain **1 resilience and 1 unphased** (a creature must sleep 6+ hours before it can gain this bonus again).

**3. Mix and match** — an alchemical brew may carry **two effects** instead of one — or, choosing one, raise its test score by 1 or multiply its duration by 1.5. Your max brews become **3 + your intellect dice count** (+1 more if your intellect is a d10 or above). Acidic cask, frosted cocktail and enchanting aroma may only be mixed **with each other**.

#### The Diplomat

*Versatile*

Diplomats master persuasion and deception — swaying whole nations with words alone.

- *Special condition — speaking terms: you only gain this tree's benefits while in conversation, not in a fight.*

**1. Proficient speak** — when convincing or deceiving a creature that is **not hostile or cautious**, you gain +1d10 as you steer its train of thought.

**2. Compelling argument** — after talking to a creature for at least 2 minutes, make a charisma check contested by its willpower: on more successes, shift its mood one step in your favor (hostile → neutral, neutral → friendly) or remove *cautious*.

**3. King's presence** *(2 points)* — you may add your **willpower or intellect** to all charisma checks (spellcasting rolls excepted).

#### The Mentor

*Support, Commander*

A master at helping others improve, body or mind — your instruction and advice always land.

**1. Proper form** — when an ally takes *training an attribute* during rest, you may spend 1 hour to upgrade it to **proper training**: the dice gained rise to a **d8**. And when an ally uses *deep understanding* or *harsh training*, you may spend an activity slot to help — they learn **1 additional** spell or technique under the same restrictions.

**2. Student and master** — if you and another character take *partner up*, that creature becomes your **student** (two mentors — one chooses to be the student). While they are your student:

- +1d6 to all hostile rolls while you're in line of sight, and +1d6 to power, speed and endurance resist rolls;
- once per round, when they're attacked within 1 meter of you, you may take the hit instead.

Lost when the *partner up* benefits would be lost.

**3. Protégé** — if you become **Ashen** within your student's line of sight, they may immediately take a turn. You also gain a camp activity, **passing on knowledge** *(2 hours, with your student)*: the student learns 2 techniques or spells you know, usable for 24 hours — or teaches you one of theirs, usable for 24 hours. And your student always enjoys **proper training** without you spending the hour.

#### The Ally

*Commander, Versatile*

Some form a special bond with beasts, people or otherworldly beings — and the trust and friendship of that bond empowers them.

**1. Companion** *(2 points)* — you gain an **ally**: a strong animal, or another mortal. You set its attribute distribution across the seven attributes: **1d8** / **2d6** / **1d6**/ **1d6**/ **1d4** / **1d4** / **1d4**. You choose its size (1, 2 or 3) on taking this talent.

Choose a **template**, one **benefit**, and one **feature**:

| Choice       | Options                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| ------------ | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Template** | **Humanoid** — equips weapons, shields and items (no inventory points of its own, but may hold a weapon+shield, two weapons, a weapon+ammo, or one long reach weapon). **Non-humanoid** — either swims and breathes underwater, *or* its short-reach attacks gain the *bladed* trait. |
| **Benefit**  | wears medium armor · +10 m movement · +1d6 to hostile moves                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| **Feature**  | **Helping hand:** allies within its reach gain +1d6 on their turn's first check. **Protector:** friendly creatures within 1 meter gain −1 damage reduction. **Battle tactics:** it may move 5 meters and attack for 1 move.                                                           |

The ally makes **1 move** in combat and acts on your turn; at the start of your turn you may spend 1 move to grant it up to **3 moves** total.
