If it would become Ashen, it is instead knocked out or flees (abuse this, and the companion may die). At camp it counts as keeping watch unless directed, and can take *searching for food*, *raising morale* or *heal up*.

**Growing the ally:** for every 2 talent points you held when taking this talent — and every 2 gained afterwards — improve it: **+1 dice size** to one attribute, **+2 resilience**, or **+3 m movement**. And for every renown rank above rookie (and each time your renown rises), it gains one of: learning **2 non-support, non-summoning beginner spells**; **+1 to one die**; or the **1st talent** of a general combat, travel or utility tree (never beyond the 1st). The ally is bound by your **renown restrictions** for dice size and count.

**2. Bonds of fate** — when a positive effect targets you (healing, a supportive spell, a beneficial talent) and your ally is within 1 meter, you may extend the effect to it as well.

**3. Loss and love** — when your ally falls to 0 resilience, it pushes through: it becomes **immune to all damage**, sheds all negative conditions, and immediately takes a special turn of **4 moves** with any number of attacks. Right after its final move, it is knocked out — and only your rest will wake it.

#### The Hawkmaster

*Commander, Controller*

Masters of the sky — befriending, taming and commanding one of nature's fastest hunters.

**1. Friend of the sky** — you learn **summon lesser sky beast**, cast free after every camp with **infinite duration** (when it dies, it simply flies off, and you may summon it again). Your beast — your **hawk**, though it can be any bird — takes up to **2 moves** on its turn, unprompted.

**2. Harrier talons** — your hawk gains a move, **blinding assault** *(2 of the hawk's moves)*: one creature within its reach becomes **blinded**. If that creature leaves the hawk's reach, it loses blinded but gains **1 rank of bleed**.

**3. Skystriker** — the first time each round a creature exits your hawk's reach, the hawk may move up to its full speed and use *blinding assault* on a **different** creature.

#### The Apothecary

*Support*

Caretakers and poison specialists — brewing antidotes and healing potions while they rest.

**1. Field doctor** — while resting, spend 1 hour to prepare **2 medical brews**, their effects drawn from the local plants:

- **Curing cream:** 2 moves to remove *poisoned*.
- **Smelling salts:** 1 move to remove *taunted* or *intimidated*.
- **Revitalizing potion:** 3 moves to remove *weakened* and *prone* — a permanent weakened (from 0 mana or lack of sleep) is instead removed for 1 hour.

Brews are administered to the holder or a creature within 1 meter, and last **24 hours** before the plants dry out. You carry up to 2 free; beyond that, every 3 formulas cost you 1 inventory point (other creatures pay 1 per formula).

**2. Medicinal antidote** — when a creature consumes a medical brew you created, they recover **2 unphased**.

**3. Specialist botanist** — when you create a medical brew, you may roll an **intellect or sense check**: for every **2 successes**, choose one benefit:

- The unphased recovered increases by 1.
- Curing cream also removes *blinded*.
- Smelling salts may also remove *unaware*.
- Revitalizing potion also removes *restrained*.
- The brew costs 1 move less to use (to a minimum of 0).

#### The Infiltrator

*Versatile*

Masters of invasion and subterfuge — breaking into any place, eavesdropping on any conversation, recovering any document, no matter how guarded.

**1. Surmount** — your movement threshold for stealth rises by **50%** (rounded up), and you gain +2d6 to pick locks, disable traps, and thoroughly search an area for hidden details.

**2. Undercover** — you ignore any reduction to your successes when trying to hide. While stealthed, you may spend a move to **re-roll your stealth check** for a better position — this also clears any reductions to your discovery score caused by hostile moves, spellcasting or re-entering stealth.

**3. Quiet slumber** — you gain a special sleeping poison, applied by weapon, injection or ingestion:

- **Ingested:** 3 hours after consuming it, the creature falls **asleep for 10 hours** — only damage wakes it.
- **Injected:** the creature grows drowsy immediately, and cannot wake for the next 10 minutes unless damaged or rattled by a loud noise.
- **Laced** *(bladed weapon)*: a damaged creature turns dreary — it counts as **unaware** for the next minute.

#### The Fixer

*Support, Versatile*

Through brilliant innovation or magical power, fixers enhance the bodies of others — or build entirely new limbs.

**1. Enhance the body** — in a safe haven, spend an activity slot to enhance one body part of a willing creature (one enhancement per creature):

- **Enhanced arms:** +1d4 to power rolls, +1 damage with melee attacks.
- **Enhanced legs:** +5 m movement, ignores the effects of harsh terrain.
- **Enhanced heart:** +1d12 to endurance rolls, +2 hours of travel.
- **Enhanced senses:** sees through abstract cover; always aware of the existence of hidden creatures within optimal range.
- **Enhanced muscle fibers:** +1d8 to power, speed and endurance resist rolls.

Enhancements must be maintained every 24 hours via *polish armor* — unmaintained, they lose all function and must be reinstalled with a new slot. You may build **artificial body parts** and gift them; they too go limp without maintenance.

**2. Modern modification** — you may add a **one-time-use** feature to body parts you enhance (recharged whenever the part is maintained):

- **Accelerate:** when you make a move, or another creature ends its turn — move up to 20 meters (30, with enhanced legs or heart).
- **Fortify:** when you guard, reduce the damage to 1 (with enhanced arms or muscle fibers, the guard is free).
- **Delicate function:** re-roll a failed power, speed or endurance check (with enhanced senses — re-roll **any** one roll of your choice).

**3. Glorious evolution** — you may enhance up to **3 different body parts** on one creature. And enhancing the same part **twice** grants the creature one beginner spell (usable as long as the part functions; −2 mana and −1 casting move, both to a minimum of 1; rolls use the **fixer's intellect**):

- arms — an elemental spell · legs — mobility · heart — barrier creation · senses — attribute improvement · muscle fibers — condition negation.

#### The Wingman

*Support*

Helping people is what you do — in social situations, tense moments, or the middle of combat. Your allies can always count on you.

**1. Moral support** — when you help a creature with a task out of combat, they add an extra **1d8** to the roll.

**2. Advisor** — in combat, when another creature fails a check, you may spend a move to add **2d6** to their roll.

**3. Performance enhancer** — when you help a creature through *moral support* or *advisor*, you push them further: for the next 10 minutes out of combat (or the next minute in it), they add **1d4 to all rolls**.

**4. Hype-man** — when a creature succeeds a roll in combat *because of* your help, it gains **2 temporary unphased**. And when an ally carrying your *performance enhancer* d4 takes damage, that d4 becomes a **d10** until their next roll.

#### The Sadist

*Support, Controller*

Masters of disease and poison, concocting the most diabolical formulas — crippling even legendary creatures with a single drop.

**1. Sinister formulas** — when you rest, spend 1 hour to create a formula. Any formula can be **ingested, injected or laced** on a bladed or thrusting weapon (or a non-gun ranged weapon) — but each has a **preferred insertion method (PIM)** that unlocks an extra effect:

| Formula | Duration | Effect (any method) | PIM bonus |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Blood nectar** | until the end of the following round | the creature cannot regain resilience or unphased | *ingested:* lasts 24 hours instead |
| **Vinesap** | 1 hour | the poison affects speed and intellect | *laced:* the creature loses 4 mana every time it spends at least 1 |
| **Necromantic larva** | 10 minutes | the first time each round the creature loses unphased, it loses 1 move | *injected:* losing any unphased also costs 1 resilience |
| **Giant's bone marrow** | 30 seconds; removable with a move + endurance check (test score = your intellect dice count) | moving at least 1 meter makes the creature weakened until the round ends | *laced:* the weakened lasts 1 minute |
| **Shattered teeth essence** | until the creature heavily wounds another creature, or becomes Ashen | the creature takes damage equal to its power dice count ×1.5 (rounded up) at the end of each round | *laced:* all creatures within 5 meters share the damage |
| **Ashen blood** | 2 hours | the poison affects power, endurance, willpower and charisma | *injected:* the creature becomes **Ashen** for the first round after injection |

A formula loses potency 24 hours after creation. Every 3 formulas cost you 1 inventory point to carry (other creatures pay 1 per formula).

**2. Corrosive** — every time you poison a creature, it **loses all damage-reducing effects** and cannot benefit from any — until it stops being poisoned entirely (not merely when the inflicting poison expires).

**3. Seed of corruption** — a creature affected by one of your formulas carries a seed: the **next poison** to touch it within a week counts as a full administration of the seeding formula, **by its PIM**. And every hour of brewing now yields **2 formulas** instead of 1.

#### The Fortune Teller

*Versatile*

The mysterious (and often inaccurate) art of studying tomorrow — frowned upon by the new gods, for the story of the false prophecy proclaiming their failure to ascend is known far and wide. What isn't known is that they *did* fail. The first time.

**1. Prophetic dreams** — when you sleep, roll a **willpower or charisma check** (chosen when you take this talent). Every success earns you a **fate token**:

- when a creature becomes **Ashen**, spend 2 tokens — it drops to 1 resilience instead;
- when a creature fails a roll, spend 1 token to add **1 success** (max 1 token per roll).

Every **failure** hands the Qg a **doom token**, usable only against you:

- ignore your damage reduction and evasion for 1 attack (declared before the roll);
- advance your Ashen turn counter by 1 round.

A new prophetic dream only comes once **all** fate and doom tokens are spent. After 3 days, both pools reset to zero.

**2. Future visions** — once per round, spend 1 move to read the fate of a creature within 10 meters. Roll a **d4** — the fate takes hold at the start of the next round:

1. **Heroic fate:** +1d6 to all its resist rolls, and it regains 1 unphased whenever it takes damage.
2. **Gruesome fate:** all grievous injuries against it worsen by 1 (a non-hero / hero not using the grievous injury rules instead takes +1 damage from all sources).
3. **Sad fate:** −1 to all its hostile rolls — and −2 to all hostile rolls against it.
4. **Unraveled fate:** *you* choose its fate.

you may spend 1 **fate token** to re-roll the fate dice, choosing either result

**3. Fateweaver** — when a round starts, you may roll the d4 to determine **your own** fate for free. Studying another's fate can be paid with **2 doom tokens** given to the Qg instead of the move. And whenever the Qg spends a doom token, you gain a **fate token**.

## The Full Spell List

Every spell in Rise of Mortals, organized by purpose: defense, offense, control, support and summoning. Each school's starting talent defines which of these spells sit on your spell list.

### Defense magic

#### Barrier creation spells

- *Note: unless specified otherwise, a wall must be placed adjacent to the ground — and you cannot shape it: walls created by these spells are straight lines.*

##### Air shield

*Beginner · 4 mana · 0 moves\* · instant*

This spell is cast without spending additional moves, as part of a **guard**. You create a small air bubble with 3 resilience: the attack you guarded against deals its damage to the bubble first — any leftover damage reaches you as normal.

##### Earth wall

*Beginner · 4 mana · 3 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You create a wall 1 meter wide, 10 meters long and 3 meters tall, within 5 meters of you — with −1 damage reduction, 0 evasion and 15 resilience, immune to bleed. Creatures caught in its path are pushed to either side (the caster's choice).

##### Shield wall

*Beginner · 3 mana · 4 moves · 45 seconds (3 rounds)*

You conjure an astral wall of warriors holding two-handed shields. The wall is made of **3 size-2 warriors**: each must stand within 1 meter of at least one other, and one of them within 1 meter of you. A warrior cannot pass through walls or creatures of size 1 or larger. Each has 2 evasion, −1 damage reduction and 6 resilience — and the spell does not end when one is killed.

##### Aegis shield

*Advanced · 8 mana · 4 moves · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

You summon forth a regiment of ethereal soldiers to form a blockade. You summon up to **3 soldiers**, each of size 3; every soldier must be adjacent to at least one other when summoned. They cannot pass through walls or other creatures' spaces. Each soldier has 3 evasion, −2 damage reduction and 10 resilience — and the spell does not end when one of them is killed.

##### Mirror shield

*Advanced · 6 mana · 4 moves · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

When you finish casting, choose a free space within 1 meter of you: a mirror shield forms there. For the spell's duration, any ranged attack or spell attack that passes through that space before reaching its target is **reflected back at the attacker** — rolled with your spell attack roll, but keeping all the original attack's properties, damage tags and on-hit effects.

##### Thorn wall

*Advanced · 7 mana · 3 moves · 5 minutes (20 rounds)*

You create a wall of thorns and spiky vegetation — 1 meter wide, 15 meters long, 5 meters tall, with 0 evasion and 30 resilience. Creatures **pushed onto** the wall take 2 damage with the *light* and *bleed* traits. Creatures standing in the wall's space as it forms must succeed on a power or speed check (test score 1) — or be **restrained** by the wall until it is destroyed.

##### Ice wall

*Master · 9 mana · 4 moves · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

You create a wall 2 meters wide, 3 meters tall and 10 meters long. Creatures caught within the wall the moment it forms are trapped in the ice: **restrained** — and unable to act at all, if the wall covers them completely. A creature restrained by the wall escapes only when the wall is **broken**.

The wall has 20 resilience, takes **double damage** from armor destroying and fire damage — and is immune to all damage that isn't physical, fire, electric or armor destroying.

##### Obsidian wall

*Master · 11 mana · 4 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You raise a wall of dark stone reinforced with minerals — 3 meters wide, up to 7 meters tall and up to 20 meters long, with **−4 damage reduction**, 0 evasion and 50 resilience, immune to bleed. Creatures caught in its path are pushed to either side (the caster's choice).

##### Whirlwind bunker

*Master · 9 mana · 0 moves\* · 15 seconds (1 round)*

This spell is cast as part of an **intercept** move against an attack. You automatically succeed the interception — and push the attacker, plus any other creatures of your choice within 15 meters of you, **20 meters back**. Until the spell ends, the 15-meter radius around you counts as **abstract cover** against ranged attacks, and as **harsh terrain** for enemies.

##### Barrier

*Legendary · 25 mana · 1 move · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

You create a wall of hardened mana and pure willpower — 1 meter wide, up to 10 meters tall and up to 40 meters long, with 0 evasion and **200 resilience**. The wall is immune to all negative conditions and continual damage effects. Creatures caught in its path are pushed to either side (the caster's choice) — and you may knock any pushed creature **prone**.

#### Damage resisting spells

##### Spell ward

*Beginner · 1 mana · 1 move · 15 seconds (1 round)*

One creature within your line of sight gains **−1 damage reduction**.

##### Spirit shield

*Beginner · 4 mana · 3 moves · 15 seconds (1 round)*

You gain a spirit shield that reduces the **next damage you take to 0** — or place it on a creature or object within 5 meters instead.

##### Safe harbor

*Beginner · 2 mana · 3 moves · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

You create a zone of peace, 5 meters in radius around you. Creatures inside it that made **no hostile move** on their turn this round gain **−1 damage reduction and +1 evasion** while they remain in the zone.

##### Elemental shield

*Beginner · 3 mana · 2 moves · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

You place a ward against the elements on yourself or a creature within 5 meters: the target becomes **immune to the effects** of one damage tag of your choice — *fire*, *electric* or *frost*.

##### Lesser revenge

*Beginner · 1 mana · 2 moves · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 5 meters (yourself included): every time it takes damage, it gains an additional **1d4 on its next hostile move**. For every 2d4 gained, it also carries −1 damage reduction until the start of its next turn.

##### Aura of protection

*Advanced · 6 mana · 3 moves · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

You exude a protective aura, 5 meters in radius. Allies of your choice inside it gain **−1 damage reduction and +1 to resist rolls**. You cannot gain these benefits yourself.

##### Guardian spirit

*Advanced · 7 mana · 3 moves · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

You summon a defender spirit — 30 resilience, 0 evasion, −1 damage reduction. When an attack hits you, the defender **takes the damage instead**. It still takes AoE damage normally, but never absorbs AoE damage in your place. If the defender's resilience hits 0, you take **4 damage to your resilience**.

##### Force cloak

*Advanced · 5 mana · 2 moves · 1 hour (240 rounds)*

You wrap yourself, or a creature within 1 meter, in a protective layer against physical force: the target gains **5 temporary resilience** — and while any of it remains, their movement cannot be lowered, and they cannot be restrained by other creatures.

##### Death memento

*Master · 8 mana · 1 move · 1 hour (240 rounds)*

You mark one creature within 5 meters as you finish casting. The first time a **killing blow** would be performed on that creature — or it would otherwise die — it is instead immediately raised with **3 resilience**, and stays immune to damage until the start of its next turn.

##### Force projection

*Master · 9 mana · 1 move · 15 seconds (1 round)*

Choose one creature within 15 meters: it is **pushed or pulled 30 meters** directly away from or towards you, and falls **prone**. For the spell's duration, any damage that creature deals to you is reduced to **1**.

##### Greater revenge

*Master · 5 mana · 3 moves · 15 seconds (1 round)*

Choose a creature within 5 meters (yourself included): every time it takes damage, it gains an additional **2d6 on its next hostile move**. For every 2d6 gained, it also carries **−1 damage reduction** until the start of its next turn.

##### Grand sanctuary

*Legendary · 15 mana · 4 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You conjure the visage of a defensive building, projecting a 10-meter aura around you. Creatures of your choice gain **−1 damage reduction** while inside — and regain **3 unphased** when they end their turn in the aura.

##### Armor of gaia

*Legendary · 12 mana · 4 moves · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

A projection of magical armor wraps around you, or another creature within 5 meters. For the duration, attacks targeting this creature lose the *armor breaker* and *armor destroyer* traits, and AoE attacks **do not ignore** its damage reduction. It also gains **−2 damage reduction** that stacks with other reduction effects — and regains **half its unphased** (rounded down) at the start of each round.

#### Condition negation spells

##### Armored mind

*Advanced · 5 mana · 1 move · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

You — or a creature within 1 meter of you — become immune to the **intimidated and taunted** conditions until the spell ends.

##### Aura of freedom

*Advanced · 8 mana · 4 moves · 2 minutes (8 rounds)*

All creatures in a 10-meter aura around you gain **+2 to resist rolls** against the *restrained*, *weakened*, *poisoned* and *blinded* conditions.

##### Lesser protection

*Beginner · 4 mana · 3 moves · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 5 meters (yourself included): the first time it would be inflicted with a negative effect while the spell is active, the effect is **immediately cured** — and the spell ends.

##### Shield of negation

*Beginner · 5 mana · 2 moves · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 1 meter of you (or yourself): it gains **+1 to resist rolls**.

##### Gentle embrace

*Master · 1 mana · 6 moves · instant*

When you finish casting, **all negative conditions** are removed from allies within 5 meters of you.

##### Greater protection

*Advanced · 7 mana · 4 moves · 2 minutes (8 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 10 meters (yourself included). The first time the target would be inflicted with a negative condition while the spell is active, **every negative condition** affecting it is immediately cured — the triggering one included. Then the spell ends, and the target takes 1 damage.

##### Pure soul enlightenment

*Legendary · 16 mana · 5 moves · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

When you finish casting, choose one target **you know exists** — wherever it is. That target is immune to **all negative conditions** until the spell ends, and any condition inflicted on it before the cast immediately ends.

#### Anti magic spells

##### Anti magic aura

*Advanced · 7 mana · 2 moves · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

From the moment you finish casting until the duration ends, **no spell can be cast within 10 meters of you** — your own casting included. Effects of spells cast beyond the aura's radius, or cast before this spell finished, are unaffected.

##### Anti magic touch

*Advanced · 9 mana · 2 moves (consecutive) · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

You wrap your hand in anti-magic. For the duration, you may spend a move to **touch** a creature, object or space currently affected by a **beginner or advanced** spell — that spell is immediately dispelled. After one dispel, the spell ends.

##### Anti magic zone

*Master · 12 mana · 1 move · instant*

A wave of anti-magic flows through the air: all **beginner and advanced** spells in effect within 15 meters of you are immediately dispelled.

##### Disintegrate mana

*Legendary · 16 mana · 3 moves (consecutive) · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

Your hands hold an almost impossible amount of anti-magic energy. For the duration, you may spend a move to touch a creature, object or space affected by a spell of **beginner, advanced or master** level — **all spells** affecting the target are immediately dispelled.

##### Greater anti magic zone

*Legendary · 20 mana · 1 move · instant*

A wave of anti-magic engulfs everything within **40 meters** of you: all spells affecting any creature, object or space in that radius are immediately dispelled.

##### Lesser anti magic

*Beginner · 5 mana · 2 moves · instant*

You try to untangle the essence of a spell still affecting a creature or area within 1 meter of you. Roll a **casting check** against the spell's test score (beginner 1, advanced 2, master 3, legendary 4). On a success, the spell's maximum duration is **cut in half** — and if more than half has already passed, it is dispelled outright.

### Offense magic

#### Elemental magic spells

##### Avalanche

*Advanced · 8 mana · 5 moves · instant*

You conjure snow and ice and launch them in a line starting from your space — 9 meters wide, 4 meters high, 20 meters long. Each creature in the line makes a speed or power resist check, taking **7 frost damage**.

##### Breath of flames

*Beginner · 1 mana · 2 moves · instant*

Fire shoots from your mouth in a straight line originating from you — 1 meter wide, 10 meters long. All creatures in the line are set aflame, taking **2 continual fire damage** for 1 minute.

##### Call upon the eye of the sun

*Legendary · 17 mana · 7 moves · 45 seconds (3 rounds)*

You call forth the flame of the dead god from the sky, to burn away reality itself. You — and only you — are safe from the fire. Choose a 3×3 meter square within line of sight and 100 meters: a beam of pure destruction falls from the sky onto it. A creature that starts its turn in the area takes **15 fire damage that cannot be reduced**. 
When a creature takes damage from this spell, it gains an **equal amount** of continual fire stacks, that can be removed only when you exit the radius


##### Dirt blade

*Beginner · 2+ mana\* · 1+ move\* · 1 minute*

The dirt around you rises into blades of metal and stone: for every move spent casting, you pay 2 mana — and every 2 mana forms one **dirt blade** around you. At the end of each round, choose a creature within 5 meters: it takes damage equal to your number of blades. The blades crumble after dealing damage **twice**.

##### Dragon breath

*Master · 7 mana · 3 moves · instant*

You unleash a line of elemental fire, 3 meters wide and 50 meters long. Creatures caught in it make a speed resist roll, taking **11 fire damage and 5 continual fire damage** — and for every 2 successes rolled, the continual damage drops by 1.

##### Earth wave

*Beginner · 3 mana · 2 moves · instant*

A shockwave travels through the earth and erupts in a 5-meter cube within 30 meters of you: all creatures inside fall **prone** and take 1 damage.

##### Electric touch

*Beginner · 2 mana · 1 move · instant*

You wrap your fingers in electricity and attack a creature within 1 meter. On a hit, it takes damage equal to your successes — with the **electric** tag.

##### Forge the weapon that strikes down titans

*Legendary · 15 mana · 6 moves · 5 minutes (20 rounds)*

You pull the strongest minerals from the ground into a 7-meter melee weapon of your choice, floating beside you. When you finish casting — and at the start of each of your turns — the weapon may strike a creature within 10 meters of you: **20 armor breaker damage**, and the target falls prone. Once per round, when an attack hits you, you may make the weapon its target instead. The weapon has 40 resilience, 5 evasion and −3 damage reduction; for every 2 resilience it loses, its damage drops by 1.

##### Fire blast

*Advanced · 6 mana · 3 moves · instant*

You focus a sphere of flame and launch it towards a point you can see. The sphere travels **30 meters at the end of each of your turns**; reaching its destination, it explodes — all creatures within a 10-meter radius take **5 fire damage**.

##### Flash freeze

*Master · 14 mana · 4 moves · instant*

Choose a creature within 50 meters and line of sight: it takes **10 frost damage**, cannot act until the start of the next round — and becomes **immune to all damage** for that time. If a single instance of damage would exceed 10 (checked before the immunity), the ice shatters and all effects end.

##### Frost cloud

*Advanced · 7 mana · 2 moves · 2 minutes (8 rounds)*

You summon a sphere of snow and harsh winds: choose a point within 100 meters — a **20-meter sphere** of frost covers the area. Creatures starting their turn inside it take 1 frost damage.

##### Ice spike

*Beginner · 2 mana · 1 move · instant*

You conjure and launch a sharp shard of ice, attacking a target within 60 meters. The attack carries the **frost** tag.

##### Invoke the power of the heavens, conjure eternal storms

*Legendary · 23 mana · 12 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You summon a storm that covers the sky to the horizon — and you are always its center. Rain and thunder deafen everyone within a **2-kilometer radius**. At the end of each round, choose a creature under the clouded sky within 200 meters of you: lightning strikes it for **10 electric damage that cannot be reduced in any way**.

##### Lightning burst

*Beginner · 3 mana · 1 move · instant*

You store electric energy within yourself, then release it in a violent burst: **you and all creatures within 6 meters** take 2 electric damage. The damage of this spell cannot be reduced.

##### Lightning streak

*Beginner · 2 mana · 3 moves · instant*

Lightning launches at one creature within 30 meters: it makes a speed or endurance resist roll (its choice), taking **5 electric damage**.

##### Lightning strike

*Advanced · 6 mana · 3 moves · instant*

When you finish casting, lightning strikes around you: all creatures **of your choice** within 10 meters take 4 electric damage.

##### Pillar strike

*Master · 7 mana · 5 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

The earth around you forms a 3-meter pillar of stone and minerals. When you finish casting — and at the start of every round — the pillar strikes a creature within 5 meters of you for **10 damage**. The pillar has 10 resilience, 3 evasion and −2 damage reduction; every resilience it loses reduces its damage by 1.

##### Plasma pulse

*Master · 9+ mana\* · 2+ moves\* · instant*

You gather energy in your hand before releasing a destructive beam. Each time you take a move to progress the cast, choose: keep charging, or fire. Every charging move beyond the minimum costs **+3 mana**. When the beam fires, creatures in a line 1 meter wide and 100 meters long take **9 electric damage** — then the air explodes, dealing 1 fire damage to creatures within 3 meters of the line. Every charging move adds **+2 electric and +1 fire damage**.

##### Rainbow shot

*Advanced · 5 mana · 3 moves · instant*

You fire a ball of shifting elemental energy at a target within 50 meters and line of sight: an attack roll with **+2d6** — and on a hit, add **two** of the following tags: *fire*, *frost*, *electric*.

##### Shattered ground

*Advanced · 5 mana · 4 moves · instant*

The ground shakes and breaks in a 10-meter cube within line of sight and 50 meters: all creatures touching the ground in the area are knocked **prone** and take 3 falling damage. The affected ground becomes **harsh terrain**.

##### Stone guillotine

*Advanced · 4 mana · 3 moves · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

As you start casting, stones float and form a blade above you. When you finish — and at the end of every round — all creatures within a **2-meter radius** of you take **5 damage** and are knocked prone. The blade has 10 resilience, 1 evasion and −1 damage reduction; every 2 damage it takes reduces its damage by 1.

##### Storm wall

*Master · 11 mana · 4 moves · 2 minutes (8 rounds)*

You raise a straight line of dark clouds — 25 meters long, 5 wide, 50 tall. Creatures who start their turn inside, or move into it, take **5 frost and 3 electric damage**. The inside of the storm is **harsh terrain**.

##### Storm nimbus

*Master · 9 mana · 5 moves · instant*

Choose up to **5 points** within 100 meters and line of sight: at the start of the next round, ethereal lightning strikes each — passing through ceilings and every barrier on the way. Creatures within 10 meters of a struck point take **3 electric damage** — once per strike, stacking if caught near several.

##### Sub-zero supernova

*Master · 10 mana · 6 moves · instant*

You detonate two explosions in rapid succession: first a burst of fire — **8 fire damage** to all creatures within 20 meters of you — then an eruption of ice — **6 frost damage** to all creatures within 15 meters.

##### Ultimate age of desolation, freeze the world over

*Legendary · 19 mana · 10 moves · instant\**

From the moment you start casting, temperatures plummet towards absolute zero in a **100-meter radius**. Every move you take to complete the spell, all creatures in the radius take **2 frost damage that ignores unphased** — and the radius shrinks by 10 meters. From the 4th casting move onward, the damage rises to **4**; from the 8th — to **7**. When you finish casting, every creature except you within a **1-meter radius is killed**.

#### Light magic spells

##### Bolt of light

*Beginner · 2 mana · 1 move · instant*

You send out a bolt of radiant energy, attacking a target within 20 meters. On a hit, the target is automatically **blinded** and takes 1 armor destroying damage.

##### Blinding shield

*Beginner · 5 mana · 1 move · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

Choose one creature within 10 meters: the first time each round it is targeted by an attack, the attacker is **blinded**.

##### Light

*Beginner · 1 mana · 2 moves · 1 hour (240 rounds)*

You create a warm light in your hand, illuminating everything within 15 meters of you. Creatures within 1 meter of you at the moment of casting are **blinded**.

##### Lesser purity

*Advanced · 7 mana · 1 move · 15 seconds (1 round)\**

Choose a creature within 30 meters: it gains a **purity mark**. The first time it takes damage before the start of your next turn, it is **blinded** and takes 2 extra damage. And if a creature affected by *lesser purity* last round starts your turn blinded, you may spend 1 move to clear the condition and mark it anew — resetting the spell's duration.

##### Greater light

*Advanced · 4 mana · 2 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You radiate an aura of bright light, 40 meters in radius, centered on you. All creatures within the sphere as it forms are **blinded** — unless they used *change the scene* to cover their eyes before you finished casting.

##### Greater purity

*Master · 11 mana · 2 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You place an **execution mark** on a creature within 30 meters. Each time it takes damage, it gains a rank of **purity**. On your turn, spend 1 move to expend purity ranks for one of the following:

- deal 2 damage per rank expended to the target and all creatures within **5 meters** of it (this option must expend **all** ranks on the target);
- spend 2 ranks — inflict *weakened*, *blinded* or *restrained*;
- spend 3 ranks — push the target 30 meters in a direction of your choice.

##### Sunlight strike

*Advanced · 6 mana · 3 moves · instant\**

As you start casting, designate a 15×15×15 meter cube within line of sight and 50 meters. When you finish, the area bursts in burning light: all creatures inside take **4 armor destroying damage** and are **blinded**. If the spell hits no one, you may recast it for 1 move and 3 mana.

##### Sunrise

*Master · 14 mana · 5 moves · instant*

All creatures in a **40-meter radius** are blinded and take **11 damage**.

##### Word of god

*Legendary · 21 mana · 9 moves · instant*

Choose one enemy — and let it hear the true voice of your faith. It is pushed **50 meters back**, and its resilience is reduced to **1**.

##### Castigate

*Legendary · 17 mana · 6 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You emit an aura of holy power, 20 meters in radius. Enemies starting their turn inside take **5 armor destroying damage**, are **blinded** — and can make only **1 move** on their next turn.

#### Psychic magic spells

##### Mind crusher

*Legendary · 30 mana · 1 move · instant*

You destroy the psyche of a creature within 5 meters and line of sight: it **cannot use mana for the next 24 hours**, loses **all of its unphased**, and falls prone.

##### Disturbing shot

*Beginner · 3 mana · 2 moves · 15 seconds (1 round)*

Make a ranged spell attack against a creature within 50 meters. On a hit, the target is **taunted** by you — and the next time it takes damage, that damage is increased by 1 and **ignores damage reduction**.

##### Manifest nightmare

*Master · 16 mana · 3 moves · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

You evoke fear and terror in a 30-meter aura around you. Creatures of your choice within it are **intimidated** by you for the duration and **cannot willingly move closer to you** — and a creature starting or ending its turn in the aura loses **3 unphased**.

##### Mental block

*Beginner · 2 mana · 1 move · 15 seconds (1 round)*

You inject despair into the mind of a creature in your line of sight: it **cannot regain unphased** until the spell ends.

##### Nightmare barrage

*Advanced · 11 mana · 1 move · instant*

A translucent bolt of pain pierces the minds of up to **5 creatures** within 100 meters and line of sight: each loses **2 unphased** and is **weakened** until the end of its next turn.

##### Psychic burst

*Advanced · 6 mana · 3 moves · instant*

A burst of psychic energy engulfs everything within 10 meters of you: each creature of your choice takes 1 damage, is **intimidated** (test score 1 to remove) and **weakened** until the end of the next round.

##### Psychic arrow

*Beginner · 4 mana · 1 move · instant*

You shoot an invisible arrow of psychic energy at a creature within 40 meters: **3 damage, ignoring damage reduction** — but the arrow can only harm the target's **unphased**, never its resilience.

##### Post traumatic stress disorder

*Master · 13 mana · 2 moves · instant*

Choose a **heavily wounded** creature — and make it relive its worst moment of the fight. The target makes a willpower check: for every **failure**, it gains one negative condition of your choice:

- **intimidated** by you (test score **40** to remove — true trauma does not shake off);
- **weakened** for 1 minute (4 rounds);
- **blinded**;
- **restrained** for 30 seconds (2 rounds).

If the creature rolls not even 1 success, it passes out from shock — **knocked out**.

##### Tear down the mind

*Advanced · 7 mana · 3 moves · instant*

Choose a creature as you start casting: **every move you spend** on this cast, the target loses 1 unphased. When you finish, it is **intimidated** by you for the next minute — and if it is **heavily wounded** at that moment, it is intimidated by **all creatures** for 1 minute instead.

#### Gravity magic spells

##### Gravity fissure

*Legendary · 15 mana · 4 moves · instant*

You tear a hole in the fabric of reality. Choose a point you can see within 200 meters: a rift opens, and all creatures and objects within 50 meters of it are pulled **30 meters closer**. A creature that collides with a solid object or another creature takes 2 damage (ignoring damage reduction) — per collision. Then the rift **explodes**, rending space in a 15-meter radius: all creatures of your choice inside take **15 damage, ignoring damage reduction, dealt straight to resilience**. A creature killed by the explosion **disintegrates**.

##### Gravity push

*Beginner · 1 mana · 1 move · instant*

Choose one target up to **size 6** within 15 meters, and push it up to 10 meters away from you. If it hits a solid object or a creature, it takes 1 damage (the creature it hits takes none).

##### Gravity rush

*Advanced · 7 mana · 1 move · special*

You gain **+15 movement** until the end of the round — and all creatures within 10 meters of you lose 10 from their current movement until the round ends, taking 1 damage that **ignores unphased**. When the next round starts, you may pay **3 mana** to recast this spell without spending a move.

##### Gravity surge

*Beginner · 5 mana · 2 moves · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

You increase gravity in a 10-meter radius around you: all creatures inside — **you included** — count as **restrained** while in the radius. A creature starting its turn under the spell's effect loses **2 resilience**.

##### Heavy center point

*Advanced · 6 mana · 4 moves · instant*

You increase the weight of a touched creature's internal organs — then instantly return them to normal. The creature loses **8 resilience**.

##### Meteor strike

*Master · 10 mana · 24 moves · instant*

When you finish casting, a meteor falls from the sky. Choose a point of impact within 500 meters and line of sight: creatures within 10 meters of it take **25 damage**; creatures between 11 and 50 meters take **10 damage** — and every object and building in the meteor's path, or within 50 meters of the impact, is **destroyed**.

##### Linear erasure point

*Advanced · 7 mana · 3 moves · instant*

You hurl a ball of almost absolute gravity, drawing a straight line 5 meters wide and 50 meters long: each creature in it loses **3 resilience** and is pushed to one side of the line (the creature's choice).

##### Push / pull

*Master · 5 mana · 1 move · instant*

You push a target up to 50 meters away — or pull it 50 meters closer. Pushed or pulled into an object, it takes 3 damage. The gravitational magic prevents affected creatures from taking **falling damage** until the end of their next turn.

##### Shackles of weight

*Master · 7 mana · 3 moves · 15 seconds (1 round)*

You multiply the gravity of one creature or object within 50 meters and line of sight. On cast, the target and all creatures within 5 meters of it lose **4 resilience** and are knocked **prone**; moving, escaping restraints and standing up cost them **1 more move**. The target itself can make at most **2 moves** on its next turn.

##### Singularity center

*Legendary · 14 mana · 3 moves · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

You raise the pressure in the air and pull everything towards yourself: when you finish casting, every creature and object **not connected to the ground** is dragged **100 meters closer** to you. When the spell ends, the pressure lifts at once — all creatures within 30 meters of you are **knocked out** until the end of the next round, struck by G-shock.

### Control magic

#### Illusion spells

##### Ephemeral copy

*Master · mana cost: the target's talent point total · 4 moves · 1 hour*

You create a 1-to-1 copy of a creature in your line of sight — same attributes, stats and permanent equipment. The copy looks, sounds and **feels** exactly like the original, and obeys your every command — but it cannot attack, use talents, or cast any spell the original knew. The moment the copy takes damage, it vanishes.

##### False voice

*Beginner · 1 mana · 1 move · 1 hour*

You enchant your voice, changing its tune and pitch — able to mimic **any sound** for the duration.

##### Fluid mirage

*Advanced · 4 mana · 2 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You create an illusion that moves, acts and copies sounds — up to size 5 in any direction, appearing as anything you want. It is not physically there: it cannot impede movement or serve as solid cover (but blocks line of sight and works as **abstract cover**). You may command it to move at the end of each of your turns. A creature with a **d12 in intellect** sees through it automatically; anyone else may spend a move on an intellect check — **3 or more successes** reveal the illusion.

##### Land of illusion

*Legendary · 2 mana every round the spell is active · 1 move · 1 round(special)*

You unleash the ultimate fabrication of reality around you. You can fully manifest and construct anything in a 2km  radius around you. The constructs make sound, can move perfectly according to pre-set commands that can be changed at any moment, and are completely intangible.
A creature can pass through these illusions with no resistance, and can conclude they are not real as a result, but cannot roll to determine if the illusion is real.
Your illusions cannot physically interact with anything, and at the end of every round, you may expend **1 move** to extend the spell’s duration by **1 round**(15 seconds).


##### Partial invisibility

*Advanced · 5 mana · 1 move · 1 minute*

Choose one side of yourself — front, back, left or right: you become transparent when viewed from that direction, and creatures standing there cannot target you with any effect requiring line of sight.

##### Phantom sounds

*Beginner · 1 mana · 1 move · instant*

You create an illusory voice or sound echoing from a point within 50 meters — audible in a radius of your choice, from 1 to 100 meters.

##### Static mirage

*Beginner · 2 mana · 1 move · 30 minutes (120 rounds)*

You create a motionless, silent image covering up to 5 square meters, appearing as anything you want. It is not physically there: no impeding movement, no solid cover — but it blocks line of sight and works as **abstract cover**. A creature with a **d10 or above in intellect** sees through it automatically; anyone else may spend a move on an intellect check — **2 or more successes** reveal it.

#### Terrain manipulation spells

##### Cave-in

*Beginner · 1 mana · 3 moves · instant*

You collapse the ceiling over a 5-meter area in your line of sight. Creatures inside make a speed check (test score 2) — on a failure, they are knocked **prone**, **restrained** under the rubble (test score 2 to dig free) and take 3 damage.

##### Cold floor

*Beginner · 2 mana · 2 moves · 2 minutes (8 rounds)*

Choose a point on the floor within 20 meters: a 5×5 meter square is covered in a thin sheet of ice. Crossing the square costs an additional **5 meters of movement** — and if that extra cost reduces a creature's movement to 0, it falls **prone**.

##### Eternal fog

*Legendary · 9 mana · 2 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

A 100-meter radius around you sinks into fog and dark mist, granting **abstract cover to all allies**. You are always the center of the fog.

##### Field of flowers

*Beginner · 3 mana · 1 move · 15 seconds (1 round)*

You raise a circle of flowers with a calming aroma — 5 meters in radius, at a point within 30 meters. Creatures starting their turn in the field are **pacified**: −1 to all hostile rolls that turn.

##### Green bush

*Beginner · 2 mana · 2 moves · permanent*

You grow a 3×3 meter bush that serves as **abstract cover**. Creatures trying to hide in it gain **+2d8** to their rolls.

##### Innocent fog

*Beginner · 3 mana · 1 move · until dispelled*

A thick layer of mist and vapor fills a 10-meter radius around you, granting **abstract cover** — and the fog **moves with you**. The moment any creature inside the fog makes a hostile move, the spell ends.

##### Pure land

*Beginner · 4 mana · 1 move · instant\1 minute*

You calm the mana in a small area around you. Choose one of the following:
**Remove** any **harsh / dangerous** terrain in a 5 meter radius around you,
For the next minute, no harsh terrain can be created in a 10 meter radius around you, and any ability that creates such terrain has **no effect** on creatures in the area.


##### Rapid growth

*Advanced · 5 mana · 2 moves · 5 minutes (20 rounds)*

Plants erupt from the ground in a 10-meter radius around you, turning it into **harsh terrain**. Enemies who fall prone in the area gain **4 ranks of bleed** — allies who fall prone are gently pushed back onto their feet by the helpful plants.

##### Sentinel's keep

*Advanced · 6 mana · 3 moves · 10 minutes*

You summon the apparition of a great warrior to bar your enemies' path. Create a 10×10 meter square, with you touching one of its sides from the outside: creatures who start their turn inside the square are moved in a straight line to a space of your choice **1 meter outside** it.

##### Swamp summon

*Advanced · 4 mana · 1 move · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

Choose a point within 20 meters and line of sight: a 15-meter radius turns filthy, covered in muddy water — **harsh terrain**. Creatures ending their turn in it become **poisoned** (affecting power and speed) — and this poison can only be cleared by **leaving the swamp**.

##### Summoning of the first forest

*Legendary · 8 mana · 3 moves · 1 week*

All buildings in a 50-meter radius around you are **destroyed** as trees and foliage grow instantly in their place. Creatures you consider allies move through the forest freely; for everyone else it is **dangerous terrain** — and ending a turn in it means becoming **restrained** (test score equal to the creature's size).

##### World tree sapling

*Master · 6 mana · 2 moves · instant*

You summon a fragment of the world tree to aid your allies: **all harsh terrain, dangerous terrain and abstract cover** within 30 meters of you is removed.

#### Negative condition infliction spells

##### Creeping vines

*Advanced · 7 mana · 2+ moves · instant*

When you start casting this spell, choose a target you can see within 15 meters of you. When you finish casting the spell, the target is **restrained** and **prone**. For every **move** you take to continue / finish the spell while the target is within 15 meters of you, the test score to escape the restraints is **increased by 1**.

##### Despair

*Beginner · 3 mana · 2 moves · instant*

You attempt to intimidate a creature within 10 meters and line of sight: roll your casting attribute — for every success, the target is **intimidated** for 1 more round.

##### Ensnare

*Beginner · 1 mana · 3 moves · instant*
One creature within 15 meters of you becomes **restrained** by vines — until it succeeds on a power resist roll (test score 1).


##### Lesser blight

*Beginner · 2 mana · 2 moves · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

A creature within line of sight and 20 meters becomes **weakened** for the spell's duration.

##### Nature's wrath

*Master · 15 mana · 3 moves · instant*

choose a creature standing on the ground within 20m of you. Roots and gravel start suffocating them immediately.
The creature is **knocked prone, restrained**(test score of 4 to escape) and **blinded**.

##### Oblivion

*Legendary · 21 mana · 4 moves · 15 seconds (1 round)*

Every round, the first time you take a move to continue / finish this spell, choose one creature.
When you finish casting the spell, every creature within a 100-meter radius that wasn’t chosen becomes **Ashen** for the spell's duration.

##### Stinging pain

*Advanced · 5 mana · 1 move\* · instant*

When another creature makes a hostile move, you may spend a move to cast this spell. The creature that triggered the spell is immediately **poisoned** (affecting power) and **blinded** — and when it stops being blinded, the poison ends as well.


##### Sword of despair

*Advanced · 6 mana · 4 moves · instant*

You conjure a sword of black mist with a **4-meter reach** and stab it at a creature. On a hit, the target is **intimidated** by you — and stays intimidated until it spends a **whole round** with you out of its line of sight.

##### Aura of blight

*Advanced · 5 mana · 3 moves · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

Miasma fills the air: all creatures within 30 meters of you become **weakened** for the spell's duration.

##### Warcry

*Advanced · 7 mana · 1 move · instant*

You emit a roar that shakes the hearts of your enemies: every creature that can hear you makes a willpower resist roll — those affected are **intimidated for 8 rounds, minus 1 round per success** they rolled.

##### Winds of despair

*Master · 14 mana · 4 moves · 2 minutes (8 rounds)*

You conjure dark and foreboding energy around up to 3 creatures within line of sight. Those creatures start feeling they know for certain they will die in the near future, and start having visions of their imminent demise.
Those creatures are **weakened** and **intimidated** for the duration of the spell, and can only lose these effects early if they **become** heavily wounded or Ashen during the spell's duration.


### Support magic

#### Equipment enhancement spells

##### Cursed weapon

*Advanced · 5 mana · 3 moves · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

You shroud a weapon you can see in dark energy: it gains the **draining** and **weakened inflicting** damage tags. The weakened condition lasts until the end of the target's turn.

##### Enhance armor

*Beginner · 3 mana · 2 moves · 5 minutes (20 rounds)*

Choose a suit of armor or a shield as you start casting. When the cast ends: an **armor** gains +1 defense value; a **shield** gains *sturdy (2)* — or raises its existing sturdy by 2.

##### Enhance weapon

*Beginner · 2 mana · 2 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

Choose a weapon you can see: its quality is raised to **pristine** for the duration. If the weapon is already pristine or better, the spell does nothing.

##### Flaming weapon

*Beginner · 3 mana · 2 moves · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

You touch a weapon and wreath it in fire: it gains the **fire** damage tag for the duration.

##### Magus forge

*Master · 7 mana · 12 moves · 24 hours*

When you finish casting, you may create up to **3 pristine quality** melee weapons, ranged weapons, ammunition sets or suits of armor. When the spell ends, everything it created disappears.

##### Phoenix eye

*Beginner · 4 mana · 1 move · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

You enchant a ranged weapon so it never misses: its next attack treats the target's **base evasion as 2 lower**.

##### Upgrade

*Advanced · 6 mana · 6 moves · 24 hours*

Choose one piece of equipment: its quality rises by **one level** (up to mastercraft) — and it gains one trait it doesn't have, or loses one it has.

##### Stormborn weapon

*Advanced · 4 mana · 3 moves · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

You touch a weapon, imbuing it with primal energy: it gains the **electric** and **frost** damage tags.

#### Healing spells

##### Aura of grit

*Legendary · 16 mana · 7 moves · instant*

All creatures of your choice within a **40-meter radius** gain **20 temporary unphased**.

##### Aura of health

*Advanced · 8 mana · 6 moves · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

At the start of each round, every creature within 5 meters of you regains **2 resilience**.

##### Greater aura of health

*Master · 13 mana · 5 moves · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

At the end of each round, all creatures within a 10-meter radius of your choice regain **5 resilience**.

##### Greater grit

*Advanced · 7 mana · 5 moves · instant*

A creature of your choice regains up to **half its maximum unphased** (rounded up).

##### Greater heal

*Advanced · 9 mana · 4 moves · 15 seconds (1 round)*

Choose a creature within 1 meter (yourself included) and roll your casting attribute: it regains **1 resilience per success** — and regains the same amount again at the start **and** end of the next round.

##### Greater regeneration

*Master · 14 mana · 1 move · 2 minutes (8 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 1 meter (or yourself): it regains **2 resilience at the start of each round**.

##### Lesser grit

*Beginner · 4 mana · 2 moves · instant*

Choose a visible creature within 20 meters (yourself included): it regains up to **3 unphased**.

##### Lesser heal

*Beginner · 6 mana · 3 moves · instant*

Choose a creature within 1 meter (yourself included) and roll your casting attribute: it regains **2 resilience per success**.

##### Lesser regeneration

*Beginner · 5 mana · 1 move · 1 minute 30 seconds (6 rounds)*

Choose a visible creature within 30 meters (yourself included): whenever it starts its turn without having been hit since the end of its last one, it regains **1 resilience**.

##### Ultimate grit

*Master · 12 mana · 4 moves · instant*

Choose one creature within 10 meters (or yourself): at the start of the next round, it regains **all of its unphased**.

##### Rejuvenate

*Legendary · 17 mana · 5 moves · instant*

Choose a creature in your line of sight (or yourself): it regains **all of its resilience**. If it is weakened from returning out of the **Ashen** state, that condition ends — and its **Ashen exit count resets to 0**.

##### Rescue beam

*Advanced · 7 mana · 1 move · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

When you cast this spell, choose an ally within 60 meters and line of sight: you heal them **1 resilience** at the start of each round, as long as they stay in your line of sight. When you cast this spell — and as a move on your turn — you may pull them **30 meters** in your direction.


#### Mobility spells

##### Aura of speed

*Beginner · 5 mana · 3 moves · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

When a round starts, all creatures within 5 meters of you may **stride for free**.

##### Breakthrough

*Advanced · 4 mana · 1 move · instant*

You immediately move up to **50 meters**, passing through solid objects and creatures. You cannot end the movement inside another creature's space or a solid object.

##### Greater aura of speed

*Master · 8 mana · 3 moves · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

When you finish casting — and whenever a round starts — allies within 2 meters of you may **stride twice** without spending a move.

##### Instant transmission

*Legendary · 12 mana · 1 move · instant*

You push your body beyond its limits: move up to **500 meters**. If the movement ends in the air, you take no falling damage.

##### Mana dash

*Beginner · 2 mana · 1 move · instant*

You rush forward up to **20 meters** in a straight line of your choice.

##### Mana leap

*Beginner · 3 mana · 2 moves · instant*

You immediately **fly up to 25 meters**.

##### Mana wings

*Advanced · 5 mana · 4 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 1 meter of you: it gains the **ability to fly** for the duration.

##### Passage

*Beginner · 1 mana · 1 move · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

You become **immune to the effects of harsh and dangerous terrain** for the duration.

##### Pathway

*Master · 4 mana · 1 move · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

You gain the ability to **fly** — and to move **through walls and solid objects** when you stride. If the duration ends while you are still inside an object, you are shot out to the nearest empty space — and become **Ashen**.

#### Attribute enhancement spells

##### Greater wit

*Advanced · 8 mana · 3 moves · 5 minutes (20 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 15 meters (yourself included): it gains **+1d8 to all sense, willpower and intellect checks**.

##### Greater physique

*Advanced · 7 mana · 3 moves · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 15 meters (yourself included): it gains **+2d6 to both speed and power rolls**.

##### Greater splendor

*Advanced · 5 mana · 3 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 15 meters (yourself included): it gains **+2d8 to all charisma rolls** (other than spell rolls).

##### Greater stamina

*Advanced · 6 mana · 4 moves · 1 hour (240 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 15 meters (yourself included): it gains **+1d12 to all endurance rolls**, and its travel time at full speed grows by **1 hour**.

##### Increased reflexes

*Advanced · 6 mana · 2 moves · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 10 meters: it gains **+1 evasion**.

##### Lesser dexterity

*Beginner · 4 mana · 1 move · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 15 meters (yourself included): it gains **+1d6 to all speed rolls**.

##### Lesser strength

*Beginner · 4 mana · 1 move · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 15 meters (yourself included): it gains **+1d6 to all power rolls**.

##### Lesser wit

*Beginner · 5 mana · 1 move · 5 minutes (20 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 15 meters (yourself included): it gains **+1d4 to all sense, willpower and intellect checks**.

##### Lesser splendor

*Beginner · 3 mana · 2 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 15 meters (yourself included): it gains **+1d10 to charisma rolls** (other than spell rolls).

##### Lesser stamina

*Beginner · 2 mana · 4 moves · 1 hour (240 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 15 meters (yourself included): it gains **+1d8 to all endurance rolls and resist rolls**.

##### Perfect body

*Master · 13 mana · 6 moves · 1 hour (240 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 15 meters (yourself included): it gains **+3d6 to all speed, power and endurance rolls**.

##### Perfect mind

*Master · 14 mana · 7 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

Choose a creature within 15 meters (yourself included): it gains **+2d12 to all willpower, charisma, intellect and sense rolls**.

### Summoning magic

All summons disappear when their resilience reaches 0, or when the spell that summoned them ends. Three rules govern all summoning:

- You cannot have summons from **more than 1 spell** active at any time, and a summon must be created within 5 meters of you.
- When a summoned creature is hit by a *mana drain* attack, the mana is drained **from its summoner** instead.
- Summons do not have turns of their own, even when they act after you: your turn's start is the start of all your summons' turns, and when your summons finish acting, your turn ends.

#### Demon summoning spells

##### Hellraiser's call

*Master · 12 mana · 3 moves · instant*

You summon **3 disgraced warriors, 2 skulls and 1 devastator**. They all die at the end of the current round.

##### Summon annihilator

*Legendary · 19 mana · 6 moves · special*

You summon a **size 5** creature of pure destruction, lingering in this realm for as long as the blood flows.

- *Stats:* resilience 8, evasion 6, unphased 1, movement 45 m, mana 54.
- *Attributes:* power 7d12, speed 5d10, endurance 2d8, willpower 1d4, intellect 4d10, charisma 6d12, sense 3d6.
- *Traits:* **Destructive aura** — no creature within 20 meters (the annihilator included) can benefit from damage reduction. **Rampage** — when the annihilator kills a creature, it regains one move. **Anti drain** — immune to *mana drain* and the *holy* weapon enchantment.
- *Attacks:* **Claws of doom** (medium reach): 7d12+2d8 — *brutal, poison inflicting, bladed*. Always uses the *savage brawl* technique when more than 1 creature is in reach.
- *Spells:* fire blast, dragon breath, mind crusher, manifest nightmare, ultimate age of desolation.

The annihilator makes **4 moves** each round, acting directly after you. If its turn ends without making a creature heavily wounded or killing one — it returns to its prison in the furthest parts of hell.

##### Summon devastator

*Advanced · 11 mana · 4 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You call forth a **size 2** demon from the depths of its prison.

- *Stats:* resilience 7, evasion 1, damage reduction −1, unphased 0, movement 15 m, mana 10.
- *Attributes:* power 2d10, speed 1d8, endurance 2d8, willpower 1d6, intellect 1d4, charisma 1d12, sense 3d6.
- *Traits:* **Focused** — suffers no downsides from being heavily wounded. **Anti drain** — immune to *mana drain* and the *holy* enchantment.
- *Attacks:* **Destructive strike** (medium reach): 3d10 — *brutal, armor breaker, forceful*.
- *Spells:* mana dash, gravity rush, lightning burst, fire blast, flaming weapon.

The devastator makes **2 moves** each round, strides once per turn for free, and acts directly after you.

##### Summon disgraced warrior

*Beginner · 5 mana · 3 moves · 15 seconds (1 round)*

You summon the **size 3** spirit of a once-great warrior — deteriorating quickly.

- *Stats:* resilience 3, evasion 3, damage reduction −2, unphased 1, movement 20 m, mana 5.
- *Attributes:* power 3d6, speed 2d10, endurance 1d4, willpower/intellect/charisma/sense 1d4.
- *Traits:* **Spreading despair** — Spreading despair: creatures who take damage from this demon or end their turn within 5 meters of it become **weakened** until the demon leaves the battlefield.. **Anti drain** — immune to *mana drain* and the *holy* enchantment.
- *Attacks:* **Touch of the damned** (short reach): 5d6 — on a hit, the demon regains up to 5 mana. (this does not drain mana)
- *Spells:* mana dash, mana leap, shield wall, earth wave.

The disgraced warrior makes **5 moves**, acting directly after you.

##### Summon skull

*Beginner · 6 mana · 2 moves · 1 hour (240 rounds)*

You summon a **size 1** floating skull full of negative energy.

- *Stats:* resilience 3, evasion 2, unphased 1, movement 15 m(hovering 2m abve the ground), mana 5.
- *Attributes:* power 1d4, speed 1d10, endurance 1d4, willpower 1d4, intellect 1d8, charisma 2d8, sense 1d4.
- *Traits:* **Spell sniper** — the skull calculates its optimal range with intellect instead of sense. **Anti drain** — immune to *mana drain* and the *holy* enchantment.
- *Attacks:* **Dark pulse** (optimal 16 m / max 30 m): 2d8+1d4 — *mana drain*.
- *Spells:* ice spike, breath of flames, gravity push, psychic arrow.

The skull makes **2 moves** each round, acting directly after you.

##### Summon war

*Master · 13 mana · 3 moves · 5 minutes (20 rounds)*

You summon a **size 4** spirit of war.

- *Stats:* resilience 17, evasion 4, damage reduction −3, unphased 10, movement 25 m, mana 27.
- *Attributes:* power 4d12, speed 3d10, endurance 5d8, willpower 4d8, intellect 1d4, charisma 5d10, sense 1d6.
- *Attacks:* **Brawl** (medium reach): 7d12 — *armor breaker, brutal*. **Killshot** (short reach): 6d12 — always uses the *killing intent* technique.
- *Spells:* stone guillotine, pillar strike, lightning strike, fire blast, post traumatic stress disorder, mana dash, mana leap.

The spirit of war **listens to no one** — not even you. It is immune to being intimidated, restrained or weakened, and always knows where the closest creature is. It makes **4 moves** each round and may repeat the same hostile move.

#### Spirit summoning spells

##### Summon Earth Spirit

*Advanced · 8 mana · 6 moves · 1 hour (240 rounds)*

You summon a guardian spirit of earth and obsidian to shield you and your allies.

- *Stats:* size 4, resilience 20, evasion 1, damage reduction −3, unphased 2, movement 10 m, mana 6.
- *Attributes:* power 3d8, speed 1d4, endurance 4d10, willpower 1d12, intellect/sense/charisma 1d6.
- *Abilities:* **Obsidian body** — the spirit's damage reduction cannot be ignored. **Bastion** — may guard against attacks targeting adjacent allies, becoming the attack's target.
- *Attacks:* **Seismic slam** (short reach, *brutal, armor breaker*): 3d8, with the **earthcrusher** enchantment.
- *Spells:* Spell ward, greater revenge

The spirit makes **2 moves** each turn, acts immediately after you — and you command it mentally, for free, at the end of your turn.

##### Summon Lesser Fey

*Beginner · 6 mana · 7 moves · 30 minutes (120 rounds)*

You summon a spirit of nature to support you in battle.

- *Stats:* resilience 2, evasion 2, unphased 2, movement 20 m, mana 5.
- *Attributes:* power 1d4, speed 2d6, endurance 1d4, willpower/intellect/charisma 1d12, sense 2d8.
- *Attacks:* **Fairy spark** (max range 30 m): 2d8+1d6 — *electric*.
- *Spells:* spirit shield, lesser grit, enhance weapon, ensnare, cold floor, innocent fog.

The fey follows you and acts immediately after your turn. You command it without spending a move; it makes **3 moves** on its turn.

##### Summon Lesser Earth Spirit

*Beginner · 5 mana · 5 moves · 1 hour (240 rounds)*

You call on rock and stone to summon a durable earth spirit.

- *Stats:* size 2, resilience 10, evasion 1, damage reduction −2, unphased 2, movement 10 m. Mana: 4
- *Attributes:* power 1d10, speed 1d4, endurance 2d12, willpower 1d8, intellect/sense/charisma 1d6.
- *Traits:* **Bastion** — the spirit may guard against attacks targeting adjacent allies, becoming the attack's target.
- *Attacks:* **Stone smash** (short reach, *brutal, armor breaker*): 2d10. **Rock toss** (optimal 6 m / max 15 m): 2d10.
- *Spells:* elemental shield, lesser revenge

The spirit makes **2 moves** each turn, acts immediately after you — you command it mentally, for free, at the end of your turn.

##### Summon little helper

*Advanced · 9 mana · 2 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You summon a little helpful spirit that tags along with an ally. When you cast this spell, choose an ally within 30 meters (or yourself) — they gain the following benefits:
- They gain +1 temporary unphased
- Every time they make an attack / deal damage with a spell, they deal +1 extra damage.
At the start of the round, you may spend **1 move** to transfer the little helper to another ally within 30 meters of you, or to yourself. The temporary unphased is gained whenever the little helper is moved to another creature. You can cast other spirit summoning spells while the little helper is active.

##### Summon messenger of the forest

*Master · 13 mana · 6 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You summon a guardian spirit that acts as a safe harbor to your allies during combat.

- *Stats:* size 2, resilience 7, evasion 2, damage reduction −2, unphased 3, movement 15 m, mana 10.
- *Attributes:* power 1d4, speed 1d10, endurance 2d8, willpower 1d12, intellect/sense/charisma 3d12.
- *Abilities:* **Magic of the earth** — the casting time of every spell this creature casts becomes 1 move.
- *Spells:* ensnare, spell ward, lightning streak, lesser blight, gentle embrace.

The messenger makes **3 moves** each turn, and acts directly after you.

##### Summon princess of thorns

*Legendary · 23 mana · 7 moves · 1 hour (240 rounds)*

You summon the protector of nature herself.

- *Stats:* size 5, resilience 30, evasion 1, damage reduction −2, unphased 25, movement 35 m, mana 15.
- *Attributes:* power 5d8, speed 1d6, endurance 6d12, willpower 4d8, intellect 2d12, charisma 6d8, sense 1d6.
- *Abilities:* **Bastion** — the princess can **guard** against attacks targeting **adjacent allies**, becoming the target of the attack. **Protection of the garden** — the princess guards for free while she is not heavily wounded. **The blood of roses** — creatures who deal damage to the princess take 5 ranks of bleed.
- *Attacks:* **Thorn whip** (4-meter reach): 6d8 — inflicts 5 bleed and restrains the target on hit.
- *Spells:* aura of speed, creeping vines, passage, rapid growth, rescue beam.

The princess makes **3 moves**, acts directly after you — and commanding her costs no move.



##### Summon Watcher
*Master · 14 mana · 6 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You summon a guardian spirit that acts as a safe harbor to your allies during combat.
- *Stats:* size 5, resilience 15, evasion 1, damage reduction −2, unphased 6, movement 0 m, mana 10.
- *Attributes:* power 3d8, speed 1d4, endurance 3d12, willpower 2d8, intellect/sense/charisma 2d6.
- *Abilities:* **Bastion** — the watcher may guard against attacks targeting adjacent allies, becoming the attack's target.
- *Spells:* gravity push, push / pull, gravity surge, pure land.
- *Attacks:* **Palm strike** (5-meter reach): 5d8 — *forceful, holy*.

The Watcher only has **2 moves** each round.



#### Beast summoning spells

##### Call of the wilds

*Advanced · 12 mana · 6 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You call forth up to **3 different small beasts**, using the stats of *summon lesser land / aquatic / sky beast*. Spend one move to give all of them the same general command — or more moves to command each individually.

##### The beast within

*Advanced · 5 mana · 4 moves · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

You unleash a creature's inner beast. An unwilling creature rolls willpower against your casting attribute — if you roll more successes, it transforms into a **lesser land, sky or aquatic beast**. In beast form it acts independently, keeping its number of moves; at 0 resilience it reverts. The creature gains nothing from talents, equipment or spells that affected its true form — and any held equipment melds harmlessly into its flesh.

An unwillingly transformed creature may spend a move to re-roll the contested check (your original roll as the test score) — reverting on a success.

##### Summon ancient beast

*Advanced · 6 mana · 7 moves · 1 hour (240 rounds)*

You summon a **size 4** ancient beast — one of the giant animals of old, the oldest life of this world.

- *Stats:* resilience 14, evasion 2, unphased 1, movement 15 m, mana 5.
- *Attributes:* power 4d8, speed 2d4, endurance 3d8, willpower/intellect/charisma 1d6, sense 2d10.
- *Attacks:* **Bite** (short reach, *armor breaker*): 5d8. **Claw** (medium reach, *bladed*): 6d8.
- *Spells:* *lesser strength* and *greater regeneration* cast themselves on the beast, free of mana, when it becomes heavily wounded.

The beast follows you and acts immediately after your turn; commanding it costs you 1 move. It makes **3 moves**, may take up to 2 different hostile moves per turn — and knows the complete **Raider** talent tree.

##### Summon lesser aquatic beast

*Beginner · 3 mana · 3 moves · 1 hour (240 rounds)*

You summon a **size 3** shark, crocodile or other large water predator.

- *Stats:* resilience 7, evasion 1, damage reduction −1, unphased 1, movement 15 m (swim), mana 5.
- *Attributes:* power 2d8, speed 1d8, endurance 3d6, willpower/intellect/charisma 1d6, sense 1d8.
- *Abilities:* **Water breathing** — survives underwater indefinitely. **Swimmer** *(optional)* — +1d8 to underwater rolls and +10 m movement underwater. **Hampered by land** *(mandatory if swimmer is taken)* — movement drops to 1 meter on land.
- *Attacks:* **Bite** (short reach, *brutal*): 3d8 — grapples the target on a hit.

The beast acts directly after you, making **2 moves** each round.

##### Summon lesser land beast

*Beginner · 4 mana · 5 moves · 1 hour (240 rounds)*

You summon a **size 2** pack hunter — a wolf, a fox, or something similar.

- *Stats:* resilience 5, evasion 2, unphased 1, movement 15 m, mana 5.
- *Attributes:* power 2d6, speed 2d4, endurance 1d8, willpower/intellect/charisma 1d4, sense 1d10.
- *Attacks:* **Bite** (short reach, *armor breaker*): 2d6+1d8. **Claw** (medium reach, *bladed*): 2d6+1d8.
- *Spells:* *lesser strength* casts itself on the beast, free of mana, when it becomes heavily wounded.

The beast follows you and acts immediately after your turn; commanding it costs you 1 move. It makes **2 moves** — and knows the **mad dash** talent.

##### Summon mythical beast

*Legendary · 14 mana · 6 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You summon the essence of one of five spirits. The base essence: **15 resilience, 1 evasion, 5 m movement, size 3** — plus one signature move per variant (it may stride before or after making it). The mythical beast needs no commanding.

- **Spirit turtle** — 50 resilience, −3 damage reduction, size 6. *Spirit's protection:* casts *spirit shield* for 1 move and no mana, targeting up to **3 creatures**.
- **Winter wolf** — 5 evasion, 30 m movement, size 2. *Ice winds:* up to 4 enemies within 20 meters take 4 frost damage.
- **Thunder boar** — 30 resilience, 2 evasion, −1 damage reduction, 10 m movement. *Storm's charge:* draw a line 3 meters wide and 10 long — creatures in it take 6 electric damage, every wall and barrier in it is **destroyed**, and the boar moves to the line's end.
- **Evening owl** — 10 resilience, 6 evasion, 40 m movement. *Nightshade:* one creature within 2 meters is **blinded** and takes 11 damage (ignoring damage reduction); if the owl moved before this, it may move again up to 20 meters.
- **Dawn lion** — 40 resilience, −2 damage reduction, 20 m movement, size 7. *Sun's roar:* all allies within 5 meters gain **+2d8** to the first roll of their next turn.

##### Summon lesser sky beast

*Beginner · 2 mana · 4 moves · 1 hour (240 rounds)*

You summon a **size 1** hawk, owl or other small flying beast.

- *Stats:* resilience 2, evasion 2, unphased 1, movement 30 m, mana 4.
- *Attributes:* power 1d6, speed 1d12, endurance 1d4, sense 1d10, willpower/intellect/charisma 1d6.
- *Abilities:* **Fly** — flies when it strides. **Flyby** — at the start or end of its turn, it may fly up to 15 meters.
- *Attacks:* **Talons** (short reach): 2d6 — *bladed, bleed*.
- *Spells:* *mana dash* casts itself on the beast when it becomes heavily wounded.

The lesser sky beast makes **1 move** each round, acting right after your turn.

#### Celestial summoning spells

##### Summon a fragment of the Holy Spirit

*Beginner · 3 mana · 4 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You summon a tiny manifestation of the Holy Spirit to assist you.

- *Stats:* resilience 1, evasion 3, damage reduction 0, unphased 3, movement 10 m.
- *Attributes:* power/endurance 1d4, speed 2d12, willpower/intellect/charisma 2d8, sense 2d6.
- *Abilities:* **Intangible** — this summon can occupy the space of another creature. **Holy fire** — as a part of the Holy Spirit, it extinguishes all impurities: any creature that starts its turn occupying the same space as this summon takes 2 holy damage.

The holy spirit makes **2 moves** on its turn, and acts after you end your turn.


##### Summon a segment of the Holy Spirit

*Master · 10 mana · 4 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You summon a sizable manifestation of the Holy Spirit to assist you.

- *Stats:* size 3, resilience 5, evasion 5, damage reduction 0, unphased 10, movement 20 m.
- *Attributes:* power/endurance 1d6, speed 3d12, willpower/intellect/charisma 2d10, sense 2d6.
- *Abilities:* **Intangible** — this summon can occupy the space of another creature. **Holy fire** — as a part of the Holy Spirit, it extinguishes all impurities: any creature that starts its turn occupying the same space as this summon takes 2 continual holy damage.
- *Attacks:* **Conflagrate** (2-meter reach; usable against a creature whose space the segment occupies): 7d6 — *holy, whirlwind*. On hit, deals an additional 2 continual holy damage.

The holy spirit makes **2 moves** on its turn, and acts after you end your turn.


##### Summon battle saint

*Advanced · 10 mana · 5 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You summon a divine warrior to inspire others in battle.

- *Stats:* resilience 8, evasion 3, damage reduction −1, unphased 4, movement 18 m, mana 20.
- *Attributes:* power/speed/endurance 2d10, willpower/intellect/charisma 2d12, sense 1d8.
- *Abilities:* **Inspiring strike** — when the warrior damages another creature, an ally that can see or hear the warrior regains 1 unphased. **Lead the charge** — when the warrior strides, up to 2 allies may move 5 meters.
- *Attacks:* **Sunsteel strike** (medium reach): 2d10+2d4 — *fire, bladed, deadly*. **Crescent moon arrow** (max range 30 m): 2d10+1d8 — *slow*.

The battle saint has **2 moves** and moves after you finish your turn.


##### Summon lesser monarch

*Beginner · 5 mana · 4 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You summon a lesser celestial to assist you.

- *Stats:* resilience 4, evasion 1, damage reduction −1, unphased 1, movement 10 m.
- *Attributes:* power/speed/endurance 1d4, willpower/intellect/charisma 2d8, sense 2d6.
- *Abilities:* **Boost** — one ally within 10 meters strides. **Encourage** — one ally within 15 meters gains +1d6 on its next hostile move. **Banish** — one enemy within 20 meters is **weakened** until the end of the current round. **Purify** — one ally within 5 meters is healed of one negative condition.

The monarch has **1 move**, acts right after your turn, and spends it to activate one ability — or to move.

##### Summon monarch

*Advanced · 8 mana · 5 moves · 10 minutes (40 rounds)*

You summon a celestial to help and command your allies in combat.

- *Stats:* resilience 6, evasion 2, damage reduction −2, unphased 4, movement 10 m.
- *Attributes:* power/speed/endurance 2d4, willpower/intellect/charisma 2d12, sense 1d10.
- *Abilities:* **Charge** — one ally within 15 meters strides. **Empower** — one ally within 30 meters gains +1d8 on its next hostile move. **Cleanse** — one ally within 10 meters is healed of **all** negative effects. **Excommunicate** — one enemy within 40 meters is **weakened** until it evades.

The monarch has **1 move**, acts right after your turn — and activates one ability **automatically** at the start of every round it remains summoned.

##### Summon procession

*Master · 20 mana · 7 moves · 1 minute (4 rounds)*

You call upon the help of heaven's full might: you summon **a monarch, a battle saint and a fragment of the Holy Spirit**.


##### Summon 𐤀̴̢̎֞𝔗̶͙̈́‡̷̜͐֟⚚̸͈̎ꙮ̶̜͒֠𐎠̷̬̌𐌊̶̠̅ †

*Legendary · half your maximum mana · 4 moves · 30 seconds (2 rounds)*

You summon- What did you summon? Is that really a servant of God? Even text cannot capture its form. Caution, that thing is beyond this realm’s comprehension, do not gaze upon it if you wish to live.

- *Stats:* Resilience: 99  Evasion: 0   damage reduction: 0  Unphased: 0  Movement: 7 meters Mana: 7 size 7
- *Attributes:* Power, speed, endurance, will, intellect, charisma, sense: 7d12
- *Abilities:* **For there shall no man see me, and live:** If this creature is within line of sight of anything, it forces them to become blinded, even if they are immune to the condition. If a target affected by this ability forcibly removes the blind condition and still has the celestial in line of sight they become a **pillar of salt**. **…with twain he covered his face, and with twain he covered his feet, and with twain he did fly:** At the start of its turn the celestial can cover itself, disabling the “For there shall no man see me, and live” ability.**…sun turned to darkness, moon to blood, stars withhold their light — end-times darkening of the sky:** The sun, moon and stars avert their gazes, for their repentance shall last eternal. Darkness falls on the battlefield for it becomes a blind spot of the gods
- **…whither the spirit was to go, they went…** - Its march eternal, unimpeded by the laws of the gods. The celestial’s movement cannot be changed or modified in any way. It can move wherever it wants, forwards, backwards, up, down, as gravity averts its gaze from it.
- *Attacks:* And it came to pass... she looked back... and she became a pillar of salt: **7d10 to hit**. 30m reach. Removes blind condition on hit.


The... thing has a number of moves equal to the number of rounds that have passed since it arrived on the battlefield

**Pillar of salt:**

- *Stats:* size X, resilience X, evasion 0, damage reduction X, unphased X, movement 0 m, mana X.
- *Attributes:* power, speed, endurance, willpower, intellect, charisma and sense: **1d2**.
- *Abilities:* **Petrified** — the pillar of salt's stats are based on the original's, X being each stat before petrification. **Repentance** — the pillar of salt cannot make any moves, as they repent. **Salvation** — if the pillar of salt becomes **Ashen**, they revert back to their original form.


## Character Template

```
Name:                     Resilience:    /      Movement speed:
Race:                     Evasion:              Mana:    /
Size:                     Damage reduction:     Unphased:    /

Attributes:
  Power:        Speed:        Endurance:     Willpower:
  Intellect:    Sense:        Charisma:

Renown:

Talent list:

Equipment:    Inventory spaces:  used / total    Inventory points:

Bio:
  Face description:    Hair color:    Eye color:
  Pronouns:            Personality:
  Backstory:
```

## Example Characters

### Cassandra Wildheart: sample frontliner

| | | |
|---|---|---|
| **Name:** Cassandra Wildheart | **Resilience:** 8 / 8 | **Movement speed:** 10 m |
| **Race:** human | **Evasion:** 1 | **Mana:** 7 / 7 |
| **Size:** 2 | **Damage reduction:** 0 | **Unphased:** 3 / 3 |

**Attributes:** power 1d10 · speed 1d6 · endurance 2d8 · willpower 1d8 · intellect 1d4 · sense 1d6 · charisma 1d6

**Renown:** rookie (6 talent points spent)

**Talent list:** Hunter 2 · Bloodletter 2 · Raider 2

**Equipment** *(inventory spaces: 3 used / 8 total · inventory points: 3)*:

- **Standard glaive** — attack 2d10+1d6, long reach, *armor breaker, bladed* (2 spaces)
- **Backpack** (1 space): 2 potions of minor health, 2 food packs, a bundle of torches, 20 meters of rope — converted from starting points

**Bio:** *(left for the player — a sample of what Cassandra could be in terms of personality, and maybe some backstory)*
